Your Class

បកប្រែមេរៀន (Translate in khmer)

👉 Seventeen /ˌsev.ən'ti:n/ = 17
👉 Number /'nʌmbə/ (noun) = លេខ, ចំនួន
👉 Number Seventeen = លេខ ១៧



👉 Inkpot /'iŋkˌpɒt/ (noun) = ដបទឹកខ្មៅ
(a pot containing ink)
e.g - 👉 There is an Inkpot on the desk. មានដបទឹកខ្មៅមួយនៅលើតុ



👉 this /ðis/ (PRONOUN) = នេះ
(You use this to refer to a person or thing that is near you, especially when you touch them or point to them. When there are two or more people or things near you, this refers to the nearest one.)
e.g - 👉 this's a book. សៀវភៅនេះ
👉 this's a Woman. ស្ត្រីម្នាក់នេះ
👉 this's an ice. ការ៉េមមួយនេះ

👉 Is /iz/​ (verb (to be)) = គឺ, ជា, នៅ
(used with he, she, it, and with singular nouns) a form of the present tense (indicative mood) of be)
e.g - 👉 she is a singer. នាងជាអ្នកចំរៀង
👉 This book is on the table. សៀវភៅនេះនៅលើតុ
👉 This is an inkpot. នេះគឺជាដបទឹកខ្មៅមួយ



⚠ ចំណាំ(Note)៖ ការប្រើប្រាស់ a និង an ក្នុងភាសារអង់គ្លេស
👉 a សម្រាប់ប្រើ ឈរនៅពីមុខ ព្យញ្ជនះ (b,c,d,f.....etc.)
e.g - a boy, a girl, a car, a dog, a cat
👉 an សម្រាប់ប្រើ ឈរនៅពីមុខ ស្រះ (a,e,i,o,u)
e.g - an ice, an apple, an egg, an inkpot

👉 eighteen /eiti:n/ = 18
👉 Number /'nʌmbə/ (noun) = លេខ, ចំនួន
👉 Number eighteen = លេខ ១៨



👉 It /it/ (pronoun) = វា
(1. used to refer to a thing previously mentioned or easily identified.
"a room with two beds in it"
បន្ទប់មួយ ជាមួយគ្រែពីរ នៅខាងក្នុងបន្ទប់(រឺ វា)
2. used to identify a person.
"it's me")
វាជាខ្ញុំ

👉 Ice-cream /ais-kri:m/ (noun) = ការ៉េមកី
👉 Ice /ais/ (noun) = ទឹកក ឬ​ ការ៉េម
e.g - It is an Ice-cream. វាជាការ៉េមមួយដើម

👉 Nineteen /nainti:n/ = 19
👉 Number /'nʌmbə/ (noun) = លេខ, ចំនួន
👉 Number nineteen = លេខ១៩



👉 apple /æpəl/ (noun) = ផ្លែប៉ោម
(An apple is a round fruit with smooth green, yellow, or red skin and firm white flesh.)
e.g - 👉 I am eating an apple. ខ្ញុំញាំផ្លែប៉ោមមួយ
👉 Is number nineteen an apple? តើលេខ១៩ ជាផ្លែប៉ោមមួយរឺ?


👉 Yes /jes/ = បាទ ឬ​ ចាស៎
👉 Yes, it is. បាទ វាគឺជា

👉 Twenty /ˈtwen.ti/ = 20
👉 Number /'nʌmbə/ (noun) = លេខ, ចំនួន
👉 Number Twenty = លេខ២០


👉 Eye /ai/ (noun) = ភ្នែក
(either of the two organs on the face that you see with)
e.g - 👉 His eyes filled with tears. ភ្នែករបស់គាត់ពេញដោយទឹកភ្នែក (គាត់កំពុងយំ)
It is (it's) an Eye. វាជាភ្នែកមួយ

👉 Twenty-one = 21

👉 Number /'nʌmbə/ (noun) = លេខ, ចំនួន
(a word or sign that represents an exact amount or quantity)
e.g - 👉 I gave him my home number. ខ្ញុំបានអោយលេខផ្ទះរបស់ខ្ញុំទៅគាត់
👉 Number twenty-one = លេខ២១

👉 Ship /ʃip/ (noun) = កប៉ាល់
(a large boat for travelling on water, especially across the sea:)
e.g - 👉 We spent two months aboard ship. ពួកយើងចំណាយពេលពីខែនៅលើ​ កប៉ាល់
👉 this is a ship. thisគឺជាកប៉ាល់មួយ
👉 Is this a ship? តើthisគឺជាកប៉ាល់មួយរី?

👉 Clock /klɒk/ (noun) = នឡិកា (ព្យួរ ជញ្ជាំង)
(a device for measuring and showing time, usually found in or on a building and not worn by a person:)
👉 We have an antique Clock on the wall. យើងមាននាឡិកាបូរាណមួយនៅលើជញ្ជាំង
👉 It is a clock. វាគឺជានាឡិកាមួយ
👉​ Is it a clock? តើវាគឺជានាឡិកាមួយរឺ?

👉 ​What /wɒt/ (determiner, pronoun, exclamation) = អ្វី
(used to ask for information about people or things:)
👉 ​What? អ្វី?
👉 What is it? តើវាគឺជាអ្វី?
👉 What time is it? ម៉ោងប៉ុន្មាន?

👉 Cat /kæt/ (noun) = សត្វឆ្មា
(a small animal with fur, four legs, a tail, and claws, usually kept as a pet or for catching mice)
e.g - 👉 My Cat likes dozing in front of the fire. ឆ្មា របស់ខ្ញុំចូលចិត្តដេកមុខភ្លើង

👉​ and /ənd/ (conjunction) = និង, ហើយនិង
(used to join two words, phrases, parts of sentences, or related statements together:)
e.g - 👉 boys and girls. ប្រុស​ និង ស្រី
👉​ We were wet and tired. ពួកយើងសើម និង​អស់កម្លាំង



umbrella /ʌm'brel.ə/ (noun) = ឆ័ត្រ
(a device for protection against the rain, consisting of a stick with a folding frame covered in material at one end and usually a handle at the other, or a similar, often larger, device used for protection against the sun:)
e.g - 👉 I felt a few drops of rain, so I put my umbrella up. ខ្ញុំបានចាប់អារម្មណ៏ឃើញថាមានភ្លៀងធ្លាក់ប៉ុន្មានដំណក់ដូច្នេះ ខ្ញុំក៏បើកឆ័ត្រឡើង
👉 it is (it's) a cat and an umbrella. វាគឺជាឆ្មា ហើយនិង​ ឆ័ត្រ

👉 Twenty-two = 22
👉 Number /'nʌmbə/ (noun) = លេខ, ចំនួន
👉​ Number twenty-two = លេខ២២


👉 OR /ɔ:r/ (conjunction) = រឺក៏
(used to connect different possibilities:)
e.g - 👉 Is it Tuesday or Wednesday today? តើថ្ងៃនេះជាថ្ងៃ អង្គា ឬក៏ ថ្ងៃពុធ


👉 aeroplane /'eə.rə.plein/ (noun) = យន្តហោះ
(a vehicle designed for air travel that has wings and one or more engines:)
e.g - 👉​ She has her own private aeroplane. នាងមានយន្តហោះឯកជនផ្ទាល់ខ្លួន
👉 It is (it's) an aeroplane. វាគឺជាយន្តហោះមួយ


👉 Twenty-Three = 23
👉 Number /'nʌmbə/ (noun) = លេខ, ចំនួន
👉​ Number twenty-three = លេខ២៣


👉 egg /eg/ (noun) = ស៊ុត
(a small oval object with a thin hard shell produced by a female bird and containing a young bird; a similar object (without a hard shell) produced by a female fish, insect, etc.)
e.g - 👉 The fish lay thousands of eggs at one time. ត្រីពងរាប់ពាន់ក្នុងពេលតែមួយ
👉 Is this an egg or an apple? តើនេះជា ស៊ុត ឬជា ផ្លែប៉ោម?

👉 Twenty-Four = 24
👉 Number /'nʌmbə/ (noun) = លេខ, ចំនួន
👉​ Number twenty-four = លេខ២៤


👉 Bad /bæd/ (adjective) = អាក្រក់, មិនល្អ, មិនរីករាយ, ខូច, ស្អុយ
e.g - 👉 Watch out - he's in a bad mood. មើលទៅ, គាត់កំពុងបង្ហាញចេញទឹកមុនមិនល្អទេ(អារម្មណ៏មិនសប្បាយ)
👉 This is a bad egg. នេះជាស៊ុតស្អុយ (ស៊ុតខូច)


👉 Good /gʊd/ (adjective) = ល្អ, ប្រសើរ, រីករាយ
(very satisfactory, enjoyable, pleasant, or interesting:)
e.g - 👉 Watch out - he's in a good mood. មើលទៅ, គាត់មានអាម្មណ៏រីករាយណាស់
👉 Did you have a good time at the party? តើអ្នកសប្បាយណាស់មែនទេនៅពិធីជប់លៀង?
👉 This is a Good egg. នេះជាស៊ុតដែលល្អ


👉 No /nəʊ/ = ទេ
👉 Not /nɒt/ (adverb) = មិនមែន
(used to form a negative phrase after verbs like "be", "can", "have", "will", "must", etc., usually used in the short form "n't" in speech:)
e.g - 👉 He's not as tall as his father. គាត់មិនខ្ពស់ដូចជាឪពុកកាត់ទេ
👉 No, It is not a bad egg. ទេ,​ វាមិនមែនជាស៊ុតស្អុយទេ

👉 Vowel /vaʊəl/ (noun) = ស្រះ
(a letter that represents a sound produced in this way:)
👉​ The Vowels in English are a, e, i, o, and u. ស្រះក្នុងភាសារអង់គ្លេស គឺ a, e, i, o, និង u.


👉 Consonant /'kan·sə·nənt/ (noun) = ព្យញ្ជនះ
(A consonant is also a letter that represents a sound produced in this way:
Except for the vowels in English - a, e, i, o, u, - all the letters are consonants.)
e.g - b, c, d, f, g, h, j.....etc.

👉 in /in/ (preposition) = ក្នុង
(inside a container, place, or area, or surrounded or closed off by something:)
👉​ e.g - What's that in your hand? នោះជាអ្វី ក្នុងដៃរបស់អ្នក?
👉 The boy is in the bed. ក្មេងប្រុសនៅ ក្នុង(លើ)គ្រែ


👉 cup /kʌp/ (noun) = ពែង
(a small, round container, often with a handle, used for drinking tea, coffee, etc.:)
👉​ e.g - a cup and saucer. ពែងនិងចានទ្រនាប់ពែង
👉 a coffee cup. ពែងកាហ្វេ
👉 the egg cup. ពែងដាក់ស៊ុត


👉 boy /bɔi/ (noun) = ក្មេងប្រុស
(a male child or, more generally, a male of any age:)
👉​ e.g - a some boys were playing football in the schoolyard. ក្មេងប្រុសមួយចំនួនលេងបាល់ទាត់ក្នុងទីឃ្លាសាលា
👉 The boy is in the bed. ក្មេងប្រុសនៅ ក្នុង(លើ)គ្រែ


👉 bed /bed/ (noun) = គ្រែ
(a large, rectangular piece of furniture, often with four legs, used for sleeping on:)
👉​ e.g - He likes to have breakfast in bed on a Saturday morning. គាត់ចូលចិត្តបរិភោគអាហារពេលព្រឹកនៅក្នុង(លើ) គ្រែ នៅព្រឹកថ្ងៃសៅរ៌
👉 The boy is in the bed. ក្មេងប្រុសនៅ ក្នុង(លើ) គ្រែ


👉 girl /gə:l/ (noun) = ក្មេងស្រី
(a female child or young woman, especially one still at school:)
👉​ e.g - We have two girls. ពួកយើងមានកូនស្រីពីរនាក់
👉 The girl is in the classroom. ក្មេងស្រីនៅក្នុងថ្នាក់រៀន


👉 classroom /ˈklɑːs.ruːm/ (noun) = ថ្នាក់រៀន
(a room in a school or college where groups of students are taught:)
👉​ e.g - All students are expected to be quiet and obedient in the classroom. សិស្សទាំងអស់ធ្វើការគោរពដោយស្ងៀមស្ងាត់នឹងស្តាប់បង្គាប់នៅក្នុង ថ្នាក់រៀន
👉 The girl is in the classroom. ក្មេងស្រីនៅក្នុងថ្នាក់រៀន


👉 train /treɪn/ (noun) = រថភ្លើង
(a railway engine connected to carriages for carrying people or to wheeled containers for carrying goods:)
👉​ e.g - Did you come by train?​​ តើអ្នកធ្វើដំណើរមកតាម រថភ្លើងមែនទេ?
👉 The train is in the station. រថភ្លើងនៅក្នុងស្ថានីយ៏


👉 station /ˈsteɪ.ʃən/ (noun) = ស្ថានីយ៏ (រថភ្លើង ឬ​ រថយន្ត)
(a building and the surrounding area where buses or trains stop for people to get on or off:)
👉​ e.g - Shall we get a​ taxi to the station? តើយើងគួតែជិះ តាក់ស៊ីទៅ ស្ថានីយ៏ទេ?
👉 The train is in the station. រថភ្លើងនៅក្នុងស្ថានីយ៏


👉 sky /skaɪ/ (noun) = មេឃ
(the area above the earth, in which clouds, the sun, etc. can be seen:)
👉​ e.g - The sky was alight with hundreds of fireworks. ផ្ទៃមេឃភ្លឺទៅដោយពន្លឺកាំជ្រួចរាប់រយ
👉 The aeroplane is in the sky. យន្តហោះនៅលើ មេឃ


👉 where /weər/ (adverb, conjunction) = ទីកន្លែង (ប្រើច្រើនជាប្រយោគសំនូរ)
(to, at, or in what place:)
👉​ e.g - where does he live? តើគាត់រស់នៅ កន្លែងណា?
👉 where is the egg? ស៊ុតនៅ កន្លែងណា?
e.g - 👉Where's the party being held?
              តើពិធីជប់លៀងនឹងប្រារព្វនៅកន្លែងណា?


👉 Question /ˈkwes.tʃən/ (noun) = សំណួរ
(a sentence or phrase used to find out information:)
👉​ e.g - Why won't you answer my Question? ហេតុអ្វីអ្នកមិនអាចឆ្លើយនិង សំណួររបស់ខ្ញុំ
👉 Answer This Question. ឆ្លើយ សំណួរនេះ


👉 Answer /ˈɑːn.sər/ (noun) = ចម្លើយ
👉 Answer /ˈɑːn.sər/ (verb) = ឆ្លើយ
(a reaction to a question, letter, phone call, etc.:)
👉​ e.g - The minister promised to give a written Answer to the MP's detailed question.
រដ្ឋមន្ត្រីបានសន្យាថានឹងផ្តល់ ចម្លើយជាលាយលក្ខណ៍អក្សរចំពោះសំណួរលម្អិតរបស់សមាជិកសភា។
👉 Answer This Question. ឆ្លើយ សំណួរនេះ


👉 on /ɒn/ (preposition) = លើ, នៅលើ
(used to show that something is in a position above something else and touching it, or that something is moving into such a position:)
👉​ e.g - Look at all the books on your desk! ក្រឡេកមើលសៀវភៅទាំងអស់នោះនៅ លើតុរបស់អ្នក
👉 The cigarette is on the table. បារីនៅ លើតុ


👉 cigarette /ˌsɪɡ.ərˈet/ (noun) = បារី
(a small paper tube filled with cut pieces of tobacco that people smoke:)
👉​ e.g - a packet of cigarettes. បារីមួយកញ្ចប់
👉​ She lit a cigarette. នាងដុត បារីមួយដើម 👉 a packet of cigarettes is on the table. បារីមួយកញ្ចប់នៅលើតុ


👉 table /ˈteɪ.bəl/ (noun) = តុ
(a flat surface, usually supported by four legs, used for putting things on)
👉​ e.g - They sat round the dinner table, arguing about politics. ពួកគេអង្គុយ តុ អាហារពេលល្ងាច ជជែករឿងនយោបាយ
👉​ The mouse in under the table. កណ្តុរ នៅក្រោម តុ
👉 a packet of cigarettes is on the table. បារីមួយកញ្ចប់នៅលើ តុ


👉 sea /siː/ (noun) = សមុទ្រ
(the salty water that covers a large part of the surface of the earth, or a large area of salty water, smaller than an ocean, that is partly or completely surrounded by land:)
👉​ e.g - We went swimming in the sea. ពួគយើងបានទៅហែលទឹកនៅ សមុទ្រ
👉​ The ship is on the sea. កប៉ាល់នៅលើ សមុទ្រ


👉 wall /wɔːl/ (noun) = ជញ្ជាំង
(a vertical structure, often made of stone or brick, that divides or surrounds something:)
👉​ e.g - We had to climb over a ten-foot wall to get into the garden
យើងត្រូវឡើងលើ ជញ្ជាំងកម្ពស់១០ foot ដើម្បីចូលទៅដល់សួនច្បារ
👉​ The clock is on the wall. នាឡិកាព្យួលើ ជញ្ជាំង


👉 plate /pleɪt/ (noun) = ចាន
(a flat, usually round dish with a slightly raised edge that you eat from or serve food from:)
👉​ e.g - There's still lots of food on your plate. មានម្ហូបជាច្រើននៅលើ ចានរបស់អ្នក
👉​ The apple is on the plate. ផ្លែប៉មនៅលើ ចាន


👉 under /ˈʌn.dər/ (preposition) = ខាងក្រោម
(in or to a position below or lower than something else, often so that one thing covers the other:)
👉​ e.g - He hid under the bed. គាត់លាក់ខ្លួននៅ ក្រោមតុ
👉​ The cat is under the umbrella.​ ឆ្មា​នៅ ក្រោមឆ័ត្រ


👉 mouse /maʊs/ (noun) = កណ្តុរ
(a small mammal with short fur, a pointed face, and a long tail:)
👉​ e.g - The mouse ran around the house. កណ្តុរជុំវិញផ្ទះ
👉​ The mouse is under​ the table.​ កណ្តុរនៅខាងក្រោមតុ


👉 dog /dɒɡ/ (noun) = ឆ្កែ
(a common animal with four legs, especially kept by people as a pet or to hunt or guard things:)
👉​ e.g - We could hear dogs barking in the distance. យើងលឺ ឆ្កែព្រុះពីចម្ងាយ
👉​ Is the dog under the umbrella? តើ ឆ្កែនៅក្រោមឆ័ត្ររឺ?


👉 Pronunciation /prəˌnʌn.siˈeɪ.ʃən/ (noun) = កាបញ្ចេញសំលេង
(how words are pronounced:)
👉​ e.g - There are two different Pronunciation of this word. មាន កាបញ្ចេញសំលេងខុសគ្នាពីរ លើពាក្យមួយនេះ
👉​ Pronunciation Drill. ហ្វឹកហាត់ បញ្ចេញសំលេងសាចុះសាឡើង


👉 Drill /drɪl/ (noun) = ម៉ូទ័រស្វាន, សមយុទ្ឋ
(a tool or machine that makes holes:)
👉​ e.g - Do you know how to use a power Drill?​ តើអ្នកចេះប្រើ ម៉ូទ័រស្វានទេ?

(an activity that practises a particular skill and often involves repeating the same thing several times, especially a military exercise intended to train soldiers:)
👉 In some of these schools, army-style drills are used to instil a sense of discipline. នៅក្នុងសាលាមួយចំនួននេះ សមយុទ្ធតាមបែបកងទ័ពត្រូវបានប្រើប្រាស់ដើម្បីបណ្តុះស្មារតីនៃវិន័យ។
👉 Everyone had to learn the emergency drill. មនុស្សគ្រប់គ្នាត្រូវហ្វឹកហាត់ក្បួនសមយុទ្ឋសង្គ្រោះបន្ទាន់

👉 Drill /drɪl/ (verb) = ខួង, ហ្វឹកហាត់ម្តងហើយម្តងទៀត
(to make a hole in something using a special tool:)
👉​ e.g He drill three holes in the wall for the screws. គាត់ ខួងប្រហោងបីលើជញ្ជាំងសំរាប់ចាប់វីស

(to make someone practice a skill by repeating the same thing several times:)
👉​ e.g The teacher Drills them in arithmetic every day. លោកគ្រូបង្រៀនលេខ នព្វន្ឋដល់ពួកគាត់👉 ម្តងហើយម្តងទៀតជារៀងរាល់ថ្ងៃ
👉​ Pronunciation Drill. ហ្វឹកហាត់ បញ្ចេញសំលេងសាចុះសាឡើង


👉 Diphthong /ˈdɪf.θɒŋ/ (noun) = សំលេងស្រះពីរ
(A diphthong is a sound made by combining two vowels, specifically when it starts as one vowel sound and goes to another, like the oy sound in oil.)


👉 Give /ɡɪv/ (verb) = អោយ, ផ្តល់អោយ
(to offer something to someone, or to provide someone with something:)
e.g - 👉 Give me that dirty plate. អោយចានប្រលាក់មកខ្ញុំ
👉​ Can you give me a date for another appointment? តើអ្នកអាចផ្តល់ឱ្យខ្ញុំនូវកាលបរិច្ឆេទសម្រាប់ការណាត់ជួបផ្សេងទៀតបានទេ?


👉 Ink /ɪŋk/ (noun) = ទឺកបុិច, ទឹកបោះពុម្ភ (print)
(coloured liquid used for writing, printing, and drawing:)
e.g - 👉 The book is printed in three different coloured inks. សៀវភៅបោះពុម្ភចេញប្រភេទទឹក បោះពុម្ភបីពណ៌ផ្សេងៗគ្នា


👉 Before /bɪˈfɔːr/ (preposition, adverb, conjunction) = មុនពេល, នៅចំពីមុខ
(at or during a time earlier than (the thing mentioned):)
e.g - 👉 You should always wash your hands Before meals. ជានិច្ចជាកាលអ្នកគួលៀងដៃ មុនពេលហូបអាហារ

(in front of:)
👉 In English, We use (an) Before vowels sound. ក្នុងភាសារអង់គ្លេស, យើងប្រើ (an) ពីមុខសំលេងស្រះ


👉 The /ðə,ðɪ,ðiː/ (determiner)
(used before nouns to refer to particular things or people that have already been talked about or are already known or that are in a situation where it is clear what is happening:)
e.g - 👉 I just bought a new shirt and some new shoes. The shirt was pretty expensive, but the shoes weren't.
ខ្ញុំទើបតែបានទិញសំលៀកបំពាក់ និងស្បែកជើង ថ្មីមួយចំនួន, សំលៀកបំពាក់ស្អាតហើយថ្លៃ តែស្បែកជើងមិនស្អាតទេក៏មិនថ្លៃដែរ។
👉 I Just bought two books and put its on the table, but now the books away.
              ខ្ញុំទើបទិញសៀវភៅពីរក្បាល ហើយបានដាក់វានៅលើតុ, តែឥឡូវនេះមិនវាទៅណា


👉 Second /ˈsek.ənd/ (ordinal number, determiner) = ទីពី, វិនាទី
(immediately after the first and before any others:)
e.g - 👉 Is Carla her first or Second child? តើ Carla ជាកូនទី១ ឬ ទី២ របស់នាង
ខ្ញុំទើបតែបានទិញសំលៀកបំពាក់ និងស្បែកជើង ថ្មីមួយចំនួន, សំលៀកបំពាក់ស្អាតហើយថ្លៃ តែស្បែកជើងមិនស្អាតទេក៏មិនថ្លៃដែរ។

(a short unit of time that is equal to a 60th of a minute:)
👉 There are 60 seconds in a minute. មាន 60វិនាទី ក្នុងមួយនាទី


👉 Man /mæn/ (noun) = បុរស
(an adult male human being:)
e.g - 👉 For a very long time, only men could join the armed forces.
              ជាយូលង់ណាស់មកហើយមានតែបុរស ទេដែលបានចូលរួមជាមួយក៏កម្លាំងប្រដាប់អាវុធ


👉 Grammar /ˈɡræm.ər/ (noun) = វេយ្យាករណ៏
((the study or use of) the rules about how words change their form and combine with other words to make sentences:)
e.g - 👉 Her knowledge of English grammar is very extensive.
              ចំណេះដឹងវេយ្យាករណ៏ ភាសារអង់គ្លេសរបស់នាងទូលំទូលាយណាស់


👉 class /klɑːs/ (noun) = ថ្នាក់រៀន
(a group of students who are taught together at school, college, or university:)
e.g - 👉 Which class are you in this year?
              តើអ្នករៀននៅថ្នាក់ ណាក្នុងឆ្នាំនេះ?


👉 car /kɑːr/ (noun) = រថយន្ត​ (តូច)
(a road vehicle with an engine, four wheels, and seats for a small number of people:)
e.g - 👉 Where did you park your car?
              តើអ្នកចតឡាន របស់អ្នកនៅកន្លែងណា?


👉 four /fɔːr/ (number) = 4
(the number 4:)
e.g - 👉 Most animals have four legs.
              សត្វពាហនះទាំងអស់មានជើងបូន


👉 horse /hɔːs/ (noun) = សេះ
(a large animal with four legs that people ride on or use for carrying things or pulling vehicles:)
e.g - 👉 He climbed onto his horse and set off at a relaxed trot down the lane
              គាត់ឡើងជិះសេះ ហើយចេញដំណើរតាមដងផ្លូវលំហែ


👉 fourteen /ˌfɔːˈtiːn/ (number) = 14
(the number 14:)
e.g - 👉 Her baby is fourteen months old.
              ទារករបស់នាងអាយុបាន១៤ ខែហើយ


👉 door /dɔːr/ (noun) = ទ្វា
(a flat object that is used to close the entrance of something such as a room or building, or the entrance itself:)
e.g - 👉 The door to his bedroom was locked.
              ទ្វា ទៅកាន់បន្ទប់ដេករបស់គាត់ត្រូវបានចាក់សោរ


👉 woman /ˈwʊm.ən/ (noun) = ស្ត្រី
(an adult female human being:)
e.g - 👉 She's a really nice woman.
              គាត់ជាស្ត្រី ម្នាក់ដែលចិត្តល្អ


👉 put /pʊt/ (verb) = ដាក់
(to move something or someone into the stated place, position, or direction:)
e.g - 👉 Where have you put the keys?
              តើអ្នកដាក់ សោនៅកន្លែងណា


👉 foot /fʊt/ (noun) = ប្រអប់ជើង
(the part of the body at the bottom of the leg on which a person or animal stands:)
e.g - 👉 I've got a blister on my left foot.
              ខ្ញុំមានពងបែកនៅលើប្រអប់ជើង ឆ្វេងរបស់ខ្ញុំ

👉 foot /fʊt/ (noun) = ខ្នាតប្រវែង (1foot = 0.3048 meter)


👉 two /tuː/ (number) = 2
(the number 2:)
e.g - 👉 They have two houses.
              ពួកគេមានផ្ទះ២


👉 food /fuːd/ (noun) = អាហារ
(something that people and animals eat, or plants absorb, to keep them alive:)
e.g - 👉 There was a lot of food and drink at the party.
              មានអាហារ ​និង​ ភេសជ្ជះ ជាច្រើនក្នុងពិធីជប់លៀង


👉 school /skuːl/ (noun) = សាលារៀន
(a place where children go to be educated:)
e.g - 👉 They're building a new school in the town
              ពួកគេកំពុងសាងសង់សាលារៀន ​ថ្មីមួយនៅក្នុងក្រុង


👉 one /wʌn/ (number) = 1
(the number 1:)
e.g - 👉 They had one daughter.
              ពួកគេមានកូនស្រីមួយ នាក់


👉 shut /ʃʌt/ (verb) = បិទ
(to close something, or to become closed:)
e.g - 👉 He shut the drawer and lock it.
              កាត់បិទ ថត ហើយចាក់សោ


👉 love /lʌv/ (verb) =​ ស្រលាញ់
(to like another adult very much and be romantically and sexually attracted to them, or to have strong feelings of liking a friend or person in your family:)
e.g - 👉 I'm sure he loves his kids.
              ខ្ញុំច្បាស់ណាស់ថាគាត់ស្រលាញ់ កូនគាត់


👉 blood /blʌd/ (noun) =​ ឈាម
(the red liquid that is sent around the body by the heart, and carries oxygen and important substances to organs and tissue, and removes waste products:)
e.g - 👉 He lost a lot of blood in the accident.
              គាត់បាត់បង់ឈាម ច្រើនណាស់ក្នុងហេតុគ្រោះថ្នាក់


👉 word /wəːd/ (noun) =​ ពាក្យ
(a single unit of language that has meaning and can be spoken or written:)
e.g - 👉 Some words are more difficult to spell than others.
              ពាក្យ មួយចំនួនពិបាកប្រកបជាពាក្យផ្សេងទៀត


👉 thirteen /θəːtiːn/ (number) =​ 13
(the number 13:)
e.g - 👉 Some people think that thirteen is an unlucky number.
              ុមនុស្សមួយចំនួនគិតថាលេខ១៣ ជាលេខដែលគ្មានសំណាង


👉 first /fəːst/ (ordinal number, determiner) =​ ទី១
((a person or thing) coming before all others in order, time, amount, quality, or importance:)
e.g - 👉 This is my first visit to New York.
              នេះគឺជាលើកទី១ របស់ខ្ញុំបានមកលេង New York.


👉 nurse /nɜːs/ (noun) =​ គិលានុបដ្ឋាយិកា
((the title given to) a person whose job is to care for people who are ill or injured, especially in a hospital:)
e.g - 👉 She worked as a nurse in a psychiatric hospital.
              នាងធ្វើការជាគិលានុបដ្ឋាយិកា នៅក្នុងមន្ទីពេទ្យវិកលចរិក


👉 learn /lɜːn/ (verb) =​ រៀន, សិក្សា
(to get knowledge or skill in a new subject or activity:)
e.g - 👉 I've learned a lot about computers since I started work here.
              ចាំតាំងពីខ្ញុំចាប់ផ្តើមធ្វើការនៅទីនេះ ខ្ញុំបានរៀន ចេះកុំព្យូទ័រច្រើនណាស់


👉 a /ə/ (determiner) =​ (បញ្ជាក់ចំនួនមួយ)
(used before a noun to refer to a single thing or person that has not been mentioned before, especially when you are not referring to a particular thing or person:)
e.g - 👉 I've bought a car.
              ខ្ញុំបានទិញឡានមួយ


👉 hammer /ˈhæm.ər/ (noun) =​ ញញួរ
(a tool consisting of a piece of metal with a flat end that is fixed onto the end of a long, thin, usually wooden handle, used for hitting things)
e.g - 👉 She took a hammer and knocked a hole in the wall.
              គាត់បានយកញញួរ មកដំទម្លុះប្រហោងលើជញ្ជាំង


👉 motor /ˈməʊ.tər/ (noun) =​ ម៉ូទ័រ
(a device that changes electricity or fuel into movement and makes a machine work:)
e.g - 👉 The pump is powered by a small electric motor.
              ម៉ាស៊ីនបូមត្រូវបានបំពាក់ដោយម៉ូទ័រ អេឡិចត្រិចតូចមួយ


👉 of /əv/ (preposition) =​ នៃ, របស់
(used to show possession, belonging, or origin:)
e.g - 👉 employees of the company
              បុគ្គលិករបស់ ក្រុមហ៊ុន


👉 baby /ˈbeɪ.bi/ (noun) =​ ទារក
(a very young child, especially one that has not yet begun to walk or talk:)
e.g - 👉 a six-week-old baby
              ទារក អាយុប្រាំមួយសប្តាហ៏


👉 lesson /ˈles.ən/ (noun) =​ មេរៀន
(a period of time in which a person is taught about a subject or how to do something:)
e.g - 👉 Losing his job was a lesson he never forgot.
              ការបាត់បង់ការងារជាមេរៀន ដែលគាត់មិនអាចបំភ្លេចបាន
e.g - 👉 lesson 3.
              មេរៀន ទី៣


👉 three /θriː/ (number) =​ 3
(the number 3:)
e.g - 👉 I've got three sisters.
              ខ្ញុំមានបងប្អូនស្រីបី នាក់
e.g - 👉 lesson 3.
              មេរៀន ទី៣


👉 third /θɜːd/ (ordinal number) =​ ទី៣
(3rd written as a word:)
e.g - 👉 the third road on the right
              ផ្លូវទីបី នៅខាងស្តាំ
e.g - 👉 third lesson.
              មេរៀន ទី៣
e.g - 👉 the third time.
              លើកទី៣


👉 singular /ˈsɪŋ.ɡjə.lər/ (adjective) =​ ឯកវចនះ
(of or relating to the form of a word used when talking or writing about one thing:)
e.g - 👉 The singular of 'mice' is 'mouse'.
              ឯកវចនះ ពាក្យ​ "Mice" គឺ "Mouse"
e.g - 👉 singular noun.
              ​នាម ឯកវចនះ


👉 There /ðeər/ (adverb) =​ ទីនោះ
(there adverb (PLACE), (to, at, or in) that place:)
e.g - 👉 Put the chair There.
              ទុកកៅអីនៅទីនោះ
e.g - 👉 he plays over there.
              ​គាត់លេងនៅ ទីនោះ

(used to introduce the subject of a sentence, especially before the verbs be, seem, and appear:)
(There is....), (There are....) មាន
e.g - 👉 There is someone on the phone for you..
              ​មានអ្នកតេមកចង់និយាយជាមួយអ្នក
e.g - 👉 There is a book on the table
              ​មានសៀវភៅមួយក្បាលនៅលើតុ
e.g - 👉 There are two girls in a classroom
              ​មានក្មេងស្រីពីរនាក់ក្នុងថ្នាក់រៀន


👉 plural /ˈplʊə.rəl/ (noun) =​ ពហុវចនះ
(a word or form that expresses more than one:)
e.g - 👉 "Woman" in the plural is "women"
              "Woman" ទៅជាពហុវចនះ គឺ "women"
e.g - 👉 To make the plural of "dog" you add the plural ending -s
              ដើម្បីដាក់ពាក្យ "dog" ទៅជាពហុវចនះ ត្រូវថែម​ -s នៅខាងចុង


👉 are /ɑːr/ (verb to be) =​ គឺ, ជា, នៅ, មាន

(a short piece of written work that you do to practise something you are learning:) លំហាត់
The book has exercises at the end of every chapter.
សៀវភៅសិក្សាមានលំហាត់នៅខាងចុងគ្រប់មេរៀន

👉 etc /ɪtˈset.ər.ə/ (abbreviation) =​ et cetera
(The abbreviation of et cetera is ect.)
👉 Use etc. when you begin a list that you will not complete; it indicates that there are other items in the list besides the ones you explicitly mention.

(a long, thin object used for writing or drawing with ink:)
e.g - 👉 My pen seems to be running out of ink - I need a refill.
              បុិចខ្ញុំអស់ទឹក ខ្ញុំត្រូវការបំពេញបន្ថែម

👉 key /kiː/ (noun) =​ សោ
(a piece of metal that has been cut into a special shape and is used for opening or closing a lock, starting a car engine, etc.:)
e.g - 👉 This is a key .
              នេះជាសោ

👉 tea /tiː/ (noun) =​ តែ
((a drink made by pouring hot water onto) dried and cut leaves and sometimes flowers, especially the leaves of the tea plant:)
e.g - 👉 I'm not much of a tea drinker.
              ខ្ញុំមិនមែនជាអ្នកដែលចូលចិត្តផឹកតែទេ

👉 saucer /ˈsɔː.sər/ (noun) =​ ចានទ្រនាប់ពែង
(a small, curved plate that you put a cup on:)
e.g - 👉 a cup and saucer.
              ពែងនិងចានទ្រនាប់ពែង

👉 flower /flaʊər/ (noun) =​ ផ្កា
(the part of a plant that is often brightly coloured and has a pleasant smell, or the type of plant that produces these:)
e.g - 👉 These flowers will bloom all through the summer.
              ផ្កាទាំងនេះនឹងរីកនៅរដូវក្តៅ

👉 those /ðəʊz/ (determiner, pronoun) =​ ទាំងនោះ
(plural of that)
e.g - 👉 Can I help you with those bags?
              អោយខ្ញុំជួយយកកាបូបទាំងនោះទេ

👉 sun /sʌn/ (noun) =​ ព្រះអាទិត្យ
(the star that provides light and heat for the earth and around which the earth moves:)
e.g - 👉 The sun rises in the east and sets in the west.
              ព្រះអាទិត្យរះនៅទិសខាងកើត និងលិចទិសខាងលិច

👉 near /nɪər/ (adverb, preposition) =​ ជិត, ក្បែ
(not far away in distance:)
e.g - 👉 Is there a restaurant near here?
              មានភោជនីដ្ឋាននៅក្បែនេះទេ?

👉 earth /ɜːθ/ (noun) =​ ផែនដី
(the planet third in order of distance from the sun, between Venus and Mars; the world on which we live:)
e.g - 👉 The sun is not near the earth.
              ព្រះអាទិត្យគឺមិននៅជិតផែនដីទេ

👉 far /fɑːr/ (adverb) =​ ឆ្ងាយ
(at, to, or from a great distance in space or time:)
e.g - 👉 Is the station far away?.
              ស្ថានីយ៏ឆ្ងាយណាស់មែនទេ?

👉 away /əˈweɪ/ (adverb) =​ ផ្លូវ,កន្លែង,ឆ្ងាយពី
(somewhere else, or to or in a different place, position, or situation:)
e.g - 👉 Just go away and leave me alone!.
              ចេញអោយឆ្ងាយទុកអោយខ្ញុំនៅម្នាក់ឯង
e.g - 👉 on the away to shcool.
              តាមផ្លូវទៅសាលា

👉 moon /muːn/ (noun) =​ ព្រះច័ន្ទ (លោកខែ)
(the round object that moves in the sky around the earth and can be seen at night:)
e.g - 👉 The moon goes around the earth..
              ព្រះច័ន្ទវិលជុំវិញផែនដី
e.g - 👉 That is the moon.
              នោះគឺជាព្រះច័ន្ទ

👉 star /stɑːr/ (noun) =​ ផ្កាយ
(a very large ball of burning gas in space that is usually seen from the earth as a point of light in the sky at night:)
e.g - 👉 We could see hundreds of stars in the clear desert sky.
              យើងមើលឃើញផ្កាយរាប់រយលើលំហមេឃ
e.g - 👉 That is a star .
              នោះគឺជាផ្កាយ

👉 picture /ˈpɪk.tʃər/ (noun) =​ រូបភាព
(a drawing, painting, photograph, etc.:)
e.g - 👉 I hate having my picture taken
              ខ្ញុំមិនចូលចិត្តថតរូបទេ
e.g - 👉 There are two pictures on the wall.
              មានរូបភាពពីរផ្ទាំងនៅលើជញ្ជាំង

👉 teacher /ˈtiː.tʃər/ (noun) =​ គ្រូបង្រៀន
(someone whose job is to teach in a school or college)
e.g - 👉 The teacher drew a diagram showing how the blood flows through the heart.
              គ្រូបានគូសដ្យាក្រាម បង្ហាញពីលំហូឈាមឆ្លងកាត់បេះដូង
e.g - 👉 There is one teacherin the classroom.
              មានគ្រូម្នាក់នៅក្នុងថ្នាក់រៀន

👉 window /ˈwɪn.dəʊ/ (noun) =​ បង្អួច
(a space usually filled with glass in the wall of a building or in a vehicle, to allow light and air in and to allow people inside the building to see out:)
e.g - 👉 Is it all right if I open the window?
              វាមិនប៉ះពាល់អ្វីទេមែនទេប្រសិនបើខ្ញុំបើកបង្អួច?
e.g - 👉 There are two windows in the classroom.
              មានបង្អួចពីរនៅក្នុងថ្នាក់រៀន

👉 close /kləʊz/ (adjective) =​ បិទ
(to change from being open to not being open, or to cause something to do this:)
e.g - 👉 Could you close the door please??
              តើអ្នកអាចជួយបិទទ្វាបន្តិចបានទេ?
e.g - 👉 The two windows are closed.
              បង្អួចទាំងពីរបិទ
(People who are close know each other very well and like each other a lot, or they see and talk to each other a lot:)ជិតស្និទ
e.g - 👉 Mira is one of my closest friends.
              Mira ជាមិត្តជិតស្និទបំផុតរបស់ខ្ញុំ
e.g - 👉 Her relationship isn't good with her father, but she's very close to her mother.
              ទំនាក់ទំនងជាមួយឪពុករបស់នាងមិនស្និទទេ តែជាមួយម្តាយវិញគឺស្និទស្នាលខ្លាំងណាស់

👉 open /ˈəʊ.pən/ (adjective) =​ បើក
(not closed or fastened:)
e.g - 👉 An open suitcase lay on her bed.
              វ៉ាលីបើកជំហដាក់លើគ្រែរបស់នាង?
e.g - 👉 one​ window is open.
              បង្អួចមួយបើក

👉 other /ˈʌð.ər/ (determiner) =​ ផ្សេងទៀត
(as well as the thing or person already mentioned:)
e.g - 👉 There is no other work available at the moment.
              គ្មានការងារផ្សេងអោយយើងធ្វើទេនៅពេលនេះ
e.g - 👉 one​ window is open, the other window is closed
              បង្អួចមួយបើក, បង្អួចមួយផ្សេងទៀតបិទ
(the second of two things or people, or the thing or person that is left in a group or set of things:)
e.g - 👉Hold the racquet in one hand and the ball in the other. person in my car
              កាត់រ៉ាកែតនៅដៃម្ខាង ហើយកាន់បាល់ដៃម្ខាងផ្សេងទៀត
e.g - 👉She gave me one book last week and promised to bring the others on Wednesday.
              នាងអោយសៀវភៅខ្ញុំ​សប្តាហ៏មុន ហើយសន្យាថានឹងយកមួយចំនួនផ្សេងទៀត មកអោយនៅថ្ងៃពុធ

👉 note /nəʊt/ (noun) =​ កាកត់ចំណាំ
(a short piece of writing:)
e.g - 👉 He left a note to say he would be home late.
              គាត់បានទុកកាគត់ត្រាមួយបញ្ជាក់ថាគាត់មកផ្ធះវិញយឺត
(a short explanation or an extra piece of information that is given at the bottom of a page, at the back of a book, etc.:) ចំនុចកត់ចំណាំ
e.g - 👉 For more information see Note 3.
              សម្រាប់លំអិតបន្តែមមើកកាកត់ចំណាំត្រង់ចំនុច​ ទី៣

👉 Exception /ɪkˈsep.ʃən/ (noun) =​ លើកលែង (ករណីលើកលែង)
(someone or something that is not included in a rule, group, or list or that does not behave in the expected way:)
e.g - 👉 Men are usually quite good at map-reading but Tim is the Exception.
              បុរសទាំងនោះពូកែមើលផែនទីណាស់លើកលែងតែ Tim ម្នាក់ចេញ
👉 Except /ɪkˈsept/ (preposition, conjunction) = លើកលែងតែ
e.g - 👉 All the students are good in english except one.
              សិស្សទាំងអស់ពូកែអង់គ្លេស​ លើកលែងតែម្នាក់

👉 affirmative /əˈfɜː.mə.tɪv/ (adjective) =​ ស្រប (ស្របតាម)
(relating to a statement that shows agreement or says "yes":)
e.g - 👉 He replied in the affirmative.
              គាត់ឆ្លើយយល់ព្រម(ស្របតាម)
e.g - 👉 an affirmative answer
              ចម្លើយ​ ស្រប

👉 interrogative /ˌɪn.təˈrɒɡ.ə.tɪv/ (noun) =​ សំនូរ (សម្រាប់ពាក្យឬឈ្លា ជាប្រយោគសំនួរ)
(a word or sentence used when asking a question:)
e.g - 👉 "Who" and "why" are interrogatives.
              "Who" និង "why" ជាពាក្យសម្រាប់ចោទសូរ
e.g - 👉 an interrogatives sentence
              ប្រយោគ​ សំនួរ

👉 negative /ˈneɡ.ə.tɪv/ (adjective) =​ បដិសេធ (មិនស្រប, អវិជ្ជមាន)
(expressing "no":)
e.g - 👉 We received a negative answer to our request.
              ការស្នើសុំរបស់ពួកយើងបានទទួលចម្លើយបដិសេធ
e.g - 👉 negative sentence
              ប្រយោគ​ បដិសេធ

👉 for /fɔːr/ (preposition) =​ សម្រាប់
(intended to be given to:)
e.g - 👉 I've bought a few clothes for the new baby.
              ខ្ញុំបានទិញសំលៀកបំពាក់ថ្មីសម្រាប់ទារកទើបចាប់កំណើត
e.g - 👉 Here's a present for you.
              នេះជាកាដូ​ សម្រាប់អ្នក

👉 example /ɪɡˈzɑːmpl/ (noun) =​ ឧទាហរណ៏
(something that is typical of the group of things that you are talking about:)
e.g - 👉 Let's look at an example of what he means.
              តោះមើលឧទាហរណ៏នៅអ្វីដែលគាត់និយាយ
(someone or something that is very good and should be copied:) ជាគំរូ
e.g - 👉 He is a very good example to the rest of the class.
              គាត់ជាសិស្ស​ គំរូល្អដល់សិស្សដទៃក្នុងថ្នាក់

👉 they /ðeɪ/ (pronoun) =​ ពួកគាត់, ពួកវា
(used as the subject of a verb to refer to people, animals, or things already mentioned or, more generally, to a group of people not clearly described:)
e.g - 👉 Where are my glasses? They were on the table a minute ago
              វ៉ែនតាខ្ញុំទៅណាហើយ, មុននេះបន្តិចវានៅលើតុ
e.g - 👉 They are all the students.
              ពួកគាត់ជា​ សិស្ស

👉 pencil /ˈpen.səl/ (noun) =​ ខ្មៅដៃ
(a long, thin object, usually made of wood, for writing or drawing, with a sharp black or coloured point at one end:)
e.g - 👉 pens and pencil
              បុិច និងខ្មៅដៃ
e.g - 👉 an eyebrow pencil
              ​ ប្រដាប់គូសចញ្ជើម

👉 an /æn/ (determiner) =​ (សម្រាប់ប្រើនៅពីមុខសំលេងស្រះ (ឯកវចនះ))
(used instead of "a" when the following word begins with a vowel sound:)
e.g - 👉 an orange
              ផ្លែក្រូចមួយ
e.g - 👉 an​ apple
              ផ្លែប៉ោម​ មួយ

👉 make /meɪk/ (verb) =​ ធ្វើ, ផលិត ឬ បង្កើត (អ្វីមួយ)
(to produce something, often using a particular substance or material:)
e.g - 👉​ Do you want me to make some coffee?
              តើអ្នកត្រូវការអោយខ្ញុំធ្វើ(ឆុង)កាហ្វេអោយទេ?
e.g - 👉​​ She make​s all her own clothes
              នាង​ ផលិតសំលៀកបំពាក់ទាំងអស់ដោយខ្លួនឯង

👉 dictation /dɪkˈteɪ.ʃən/ (noun) =​ សរសេរតាមអាន
(a test in which a piece of writing is dictated to students learning a foreign language, to test their ability to hear and write the language correctly:)
e.g - 👉​ Our english dictation lasted half an hour.
              ការសរសរតាមអានភាសារអង់គ្លេសកន្លះម៉ោងចុងក្រោយ
e.g - 👉​​ I'll ask my assistant to take dictation
              ខ្ញុំនឹងអោយជំនួយការ​ សរសេរតាមខ្ញុំប្រាប់

👉 fourth /fɔːθ/ (ordinal number) =​ ទី៤
(4th written as a word:)
e.g - 👉​ My birthday is on the fourth (of December)
              ថ្ងៃខួបកំណើតខ្ញុំគឺទី៤ខែធ្នូ
e.g - 👉​​ Mark finished fourth in the race.
              mark បាន​ ទី៤ក្នុងការប្រណាំង

👉 he /hiː/ (pronoun) =​ គាត់, វា (ប្រុស)
(used as the subject of a verb to refer to a man, boy, or male animal that has already been mentioned:)
e.g - 👉Don't ask Andrew, he won't know.
              កុំសួរ Andrewគាត់មិនដឹងទេ
e.g - 👉​​ There's no need to be frightened - he's a very friendly dog.
              មិនចាំបាច់ខ្លាយទេ ឆ្កែនេះ​ វាស្លូតទេ

👉 she /ʃiː/ (pronoun) =​ គាត់, នាង,វា (ស្រី)
(used as the subject of a verb to refer to a woman, girl, or female animal that has already been mentioned:)
e.g - 👉I asked my mother if she'd lend me some money, but she said no
              ខ្ញុំបានសួរម្តាយខ្ញុំដើម្បីខ្ចីលុយមួយចំនួនតែគាត់មិនអោយ
e.g - 👉​​ If I tell Marie she might tell Jane.
              ប្រសិនបើខ្ញុំប្រាប់ Marie​ នាងប្រាកដជាប្រាប់ Jane

👉 chair /tʃeər/ (noun) =​ កៅអី
(a seat for one person that has a back, usually four legs, and sometimes two arms)
e.g - 👉Don't tip your chair back like that, you'll fall.
              កុំផ្អៀងកៅអីទៅក្រោយដូចនេះ អ្នកអាចដួល
((the official position of) a person in charge of a meeting, official group or organization:)
ផ្លាស់ប្តូតំណែង
e.g - 👉​​ Who will take the chair at the next meeting?
              អ្នកណានឹងជំនួសតំណែងប្រធាននៅកិច្ចប្រជុំបន្ទាប់

👉 mr /ˈmɪs.tər/ (noun) =​ លោក (ប្រុស)
(a title used before the family name or full name of a man who has no other title, or when talking to man who holds a particular official position:)
e.g - 👉Have you met mr Kennedy?
              អ្នកបានជួបលោក kennedy ទេ?
e.g - 👉​​ Mr Brown.
              លោក Brown

👉 father /ˈfɑː.ðər/ (noun) =​ ឪពុក
(a male parent:)
e.g - 👉My father took me to watch the football every Saturday.
              ឪពុក របស់ខ្ញុំ នាំខ្ញុំទៅមើលបាល់ទាត់រាល់ថ្ងៃសៅរ៏
e.g - 👉The children's father came to pick them up from school.
              ឪពុក របស់ក្មេងៗ មកទទួពួកគាត់ចេញពីសាលា
e.g - 👉My father retired seven years ago.
              ឪពុក របស់ខ្ញុំចូលនិវត្តន៏ 7ឆ្នាំហើយ

👉 son /sʌn/ (noun) =​ កូនប្រុស
(your male child:)
e.g - 👉This is our son santong.
              នេះគឺជាកូនប្រុស របស់ពួកយើង santong
e.g - 👉We have two sons and three daughters.
              ពួកយើងមានកូនប្រុស ពីរនាក់ និង​ កូនស្រីបីនាក់
e.g - 👉I have two sons.
              ខ្ញុំមានកូនប្រុស ពីរនាក់

👉 Mrs /ˈmɪs.ɪz/ (noun) =​ លោកស្រី, អ្នកស្រី
(a title used before the family name or full name of a married woman who has no other title:)
e.g - 👉Hello, Mrs brown, how are you to day?
              សួរស្តីអ្នកស្រី brown, សុខសប្បាយទេថ្ងៃនេះ?

wives plural of wife

👉 wife /waɪf/ (noun) =​ ប្រពន្ឋ, ភរិយា
(the woman that you are married to:)

              នាងជាប្រពន្ឋ ទី3របស់គាត់

(the man that you are married to:)
e.g - 👉I've never met mrs brown's husband.
              ខ្ញុំមិនដែលបានជួបប្តី របស់អ្នកស្រីbrown សោះ

👉 mother/ˈmʌð.ər/ (noun) =​ ម្តាយ

              ម្តាយ របស់ខ្ញុំរៀបការនៅអាយុ21
e.g - 👉may i borrow your car, mother?
              ម៉ែ អោយខ្ញុំខ្ចីឡានជិះសិនមក?
e.g - 👉All the mothers​ and fathers had been invited to the end-of-term concert.
              ម្តាយ និង ឪពុកគ្រប់រូបត្រូវបានអញ្ចើញ ចូលរួមការប្រគុំតន្ត្រីចុងក្រោយ
e.g - 👉The little kittens and their mother​ were all curled up asleep in the same basket.
              កូនឆ្មាតូចៗហើយនិងម្តាយ របស់ពួកវាដេកសណ្តូកខ្លួនជាមួយគ្នាក្នុងកន្ត្រកតែមួយ

👉 daughter/ˈdɔː.tər/ (noun) =​ កូនស្រី
(your female child:)

👉 sister /ˈsɪs.tər/ (noun) =​ បងប្អូនស្រី

              Lynn ចាត់ជាមិត្តល្អម្នាក់ - នាងចាត់ទុកខ្ញុំដួចជាប្អូនស្រី
(a woman who shares an interest with you, especially that of improving women's rights:)

              យើងត្រូវតែប្រយុទ្ឋតតាំងសម្រាប់សិទ្ឋជានារី
(a female nurse who is in charge of a department of a hospital:)

              នារីបម្រើកា បានប្រាប់យើងថាម៉ោងទស្សនាបានចប់ហើយ
👉 sister /ˈsɪs.tər/ (adj) [use before noun]

👉 brother /ˈbrʌð.ər/ (noun) =​ បងប្អូនប្រុស
(a man or boy with the same parents as another person:)

              តើអ្នកមានបងប្អូនប្រុស​ និងបងប្អូនស្រីទេ?

(a man who is a member of the same group as you or who shares an interest with you or has a similar way of thinking to you:)
e.g - 👉"Let us unite, brothers and fight this unjust law!"
              ពួកយើងរួមសាមគ្គីគ្នា និងប្រយុទ្ឋប្រឆាំងច្បាប់អយុត្តិធម៌នេះ
(used as the title of a man, such as a monk, who belongs to a religious organization:)
e.g - 👉Brother Michael and Brother John were deep in conversation.
              Brother Michael and Brother John សន្ទនាគ្នាស៊ីជម្រៅ
👉 Bless you, Brother.
              ជូនពរ brother
(used to express annoyance or surprise:)
e.g - 👉Oh, brother, are we in a mess now!
              អូ! brother, យើងកំពុងបង្កើតភាពរញ៉េរញ៉ាំហើយ

👉 sixteen /ˌsɪkˈstiːn/ (number) =​ 16 (ដប់ប្រាំមួយ)
(the number 16:)
e.g - 👉We have got sixteen (people) coming for lunch.
              យើងមានមនុស្សចំនួយ16​ នាក់មកចូលរួមអាហារពេលថ្ងៃ
👉 sixteenth /ˌsɪkˈstiːnθ/ (ordinal number) =​ ទី16 (ទីដប់ប្រាំមួយ)
e.g - 👉Their anniversary is on the sixteenth ​ (of June).
              បុណ្យខួបពួកយើងនៅថ្ងៃ ទី១៦(ខែ មិថុនា)

👉 subject /ˈsʌb.dʒekt/ (noun) (AREA OF DISCUSSION) =​ ប្រធានបទ
(the thing that is being discussed, considered, or studied:)
e.g - 👉Our subject for discussion is homelessness.
              ប្រធានបទ​ ដែលលើកមកជជែកពិភាគសា គឺភាពកង្វះខាតផ្ទះសម្បែង
e.g -👉She has made a series of documentaries on the subject of family relationships.
              នាងបានផលិតចងក្រងភាពយន្តឯកសារតាមលំដាប់បន្តបន្តាប់ លើ ប្រធានបទទំនាក់ទំនងរវាងសាច់ញាតិក្នុងគ្រួរសារ
👉 subject /ˈsʌb.dʒekt/ (noun) (AREA OF STUDY) =​ មុខវិជ្ជា
(an area of knowledge that is studied in school, college, or university:)
e.g -👉My favourite subject at school were history and English.
               មុខវិជ្ជាដែលខ្ញុំចូលចិត្តរៀននៅសាលាគឺ ប្រវត្តសាស្ត្រ និង ភាសារអង់គ្លេស
(to start talking about a different subject:)
e.g -👉I'd tried to explain the situation, but he just changed the subject.
              ខ្ញុំបានព្យាយាមពន្យល់នូវស្ថានភាពជាក់ស្តែង,​ ប៉ុន្តែគាត់បែជានិយាយ ផ្សេងទៅវិញ
👉 subject /ˈsʌb.dʒekt/ (noun) (GRAMMAR) =​ ប្រធាន
(the person or thing that performs the action of a verb, or is joined to a description by a verb:)
e.g -👉"Boy" is the subject of the sentence "Boy threw the ball."
              "Boy" ជាប្រធាននៃប្រយោគ

👉 object /ˈɒb.dʒɪkt/ (noun) =​ វត្ថុ
(a thing that you can see or touch but that is not usually a living animal, plant, or person:)
e.g - 👉a collection of precious subject
              ប្រមូលផ្តុំវត្ថុមាន​ ដែលមានតម្លៃ
e.g -👉Several people reported seeing a strange subject in the sky.
              មនុស្សមួយចំនួនបានរាយការណ៏មកថា បានឃើញ វត្ថុចម្លែកមួយនៅលើមេឃ
e.g -👉A new baby will automatically curl its fingers round any subject it touches.
               ទារកទើបកើតនិងធ្វើក្តាប់ម្រៀមដៃដោយស្វាយប្រវត្តន៏ជុំវិញ វត្ថុណាមួយដែលវាបានប៉ាស់
👉 object /ˈɒb.dʒɪkt/ (noun)(grammar) =​ កម្មបទ
(a noun or noun phrase that is affected by the action of a verb or that follows a preposition:)
e.g -👉In the sentence "I play football", "football" is the object of the verb "play"
              នៅក្នុងប្រយោគ "I play football",​ "football" គឺជាកម្មបទនៃកិរិយាសព្ទ័ "play"
👉 subject /ˈsʌb.dʒekt/ (noun) (GRAMMAR) =​ ប្រធាន
(the person or thing that performs the action of a verb, or is joined to a description by a verb:)
e.g -👉"Boy" is the subject of the sentence "Boy threw the ball."
              "Boy" ជាប្រធាននៃប្រយោគ

👉 form /fɔːm/ (verb) =​ កើនឡើង
(to begin to exist or to make something begin to exist:)
e.g - 👉A crowd formed around the accident.
              ហ្វូមនុ្សបានបន្តកើនឡើងជាបន្តបន្ទាប់ ជុំវិញគ្រោះថ្នាក់
e.g -👉A solution began to form in her mind.
              ដំណោះស្រាយចាប់ផ្តើម កើតមានក្នុងគំនិតរបស់គាត់
e.g -👉I formed the impression that she didn't really want to come.
               ខ្ញុំ ផ្តើមមានគំនិតដឹងថា នាងពិតជាមិនចង់មកនោះទេ
(to make something into a particular shape:)
e.g -👉She formed the clay into a small bowl.
              នាងបានធ្វើដីឥដ្ឋអោយខ្លាយទៅជារូបរាងចានក្រឡូមតូចមួយ
e.g -👉Together they would form the next government.
              ពួកគេរួមគ្នាបង្កើតបានជារដ្ឋាភិបាលបន្ទាប់មួយ
👉 form /fɔːm/ (noun) =​ ទម្រង់
(a paper or set of papers printed with spaces in which answers to questions can be written or information can be recorded in an organized way:)
e.g -👉​ an application form
              ក្រដាសបំពេញពាក្យ ស្នើសុំការងារ
e.g -👉Please fill in/out the form with black ink.
              សូមបំពេញពាក្យនៅលើ ក្រដាស(form)ដោយប្រើទឹកខ្មៅ
e.g -👉When you have completed the form, hand it in at the desk.
              នៅពេលដែលបំពេញចប់, ដាក់វានៅលើតុ
👉 form noun (GRAMMAR)
(one part of a verb or other word that has a special use or meaning:)
👉 The continuous form of "stand" is "standing".
👉 "Stood" is the irregular past tense form of "stand".
👉 "Hers" is the possessive form of "her".
👉 "Isn't" is the short form of "is not".

👉 some /sʌm/ (determiner) =​ មួយចំនួន
(an amount or number of something that is not stated or not known; a part of something:)
e.g - 👉There's some cake in the kitchen if you'd like it.
              មាននំមួយចំនួន​ នៅក្នុងបន្ទប់បាយ អ្នកអាចយកញាំបាន
e.g -👉Here's some news you might be interested in.
              នេះជាពត៌មាន មួយចំនួនអ្នកអាចនឹងចាប់អារម្មណ៏
e.g -👉We've been having some problems with our TV over the last few weeks.
               យើងមានបញ្ហា មួយចំនួនទាក់ទងនិង TV របស់យើង បុន្មានអាទិត្យមកនេះ
e.g -👉In the sentence "I play football", "football" is the object of the verb "play"
              នៅក្នុងប្រយោគ "I play football",​ "football" គឺជាកម្មបទនៃកិរិយាសព្ទ័ "play"
👉 subject /ˈsʌb.dʒekt/ (noun) (GRAMMAR) =​ ប្រធាន
(the person or thing that performs the action of a verb, or is joined to a description by a verb:)
e.g -👉"Boy" is the subject of the sentence "Boy threw the ball."
              "Boy" ជាប្រធាននៃប្រយោគ

👉 pronoun /ˈprəʊ.naʊn/ =​ សព្វនាម
(a word that is used instead of a noun or a noun phrase:)
e.g - 👉Pronouns are often used to refer to a noun that has already been mentioned.
              សព្វនាម​ ជាទូទៅគឺប្រើ សំដៅដល់ នាម ដែលបានប្រើរួយហើយ
e.g -👉"She", "it", and "who" are all examples of pronouns.
              "She", "it", and "who" ជាឧទាហរណ៏ ទាំងអស់នៃ សព្វនាម

👉 when /wen/ (adverb, conjunction) =​ ពេលវេលា (សួររកពេល)
(at what time; at the time at which:)
e.g - 👉"I did tell you about it."​ "When? ​ I don't remember."

               តើពេលណា អ្នកនឹងចេញទៅ?

               តើពេលណា ទើបទារកចាប់កំណើត?

              យើងបានធ្វើការអញ្ចើញមនុស្ស ៣០នាក់ ចូលរួមកម្មវិធីពួក ពួកវានៅទីនេះ
(used to refer to everyone, or informally to the group that you are speaking to:)
e.g - 👉 people will think you've gone mad.​
              មនុស្ស ទាំងនោះនឹងគិតថាអ្នកឆ្កួត
e.g - 👉 Now that we've discussed our problems, are people happy with the decisions we've made?​
              ឥឡូវជាពេលដែលយើងត្រូវដោះស្រាយបញ្ហាហើយ, តើប្រជាជន ពេញចិត្តនឹងការសម្រេចចិត្តរបស់យើងទេ?

👉 after /ˈɑːf.tər/ (preposition) =​ បន្ទាប់ពី
(following in time, place, or order:)
e.g - 👉Let's go for a walk ​ after breakfast.
              ទៅដើរលេង បន្ទាប់ពី អាហារពេលព្រឹកហើយ
e.g - 👉 Some people believe in life ​ after death.
              មនុស្សមួយចំនួនជឿរអំពីជីវិតបន្ទាប់ពី ស្លាប់
e.g - 👉Her name came after mine on the list. ​
              ឈ្មោះរបស់នាងនៅបន្ទាប់ពី ឈ្មោះរបស់ខ្ញុំ
e.g - 👉 There's a good film on the day after tomorrow.​
              មានរឿងល្អមើកនៅថ្ងៃខានស្អែក
e.g - 👉 She just keeps on working, day after day, week after week (= continuously). ​
              នាងធ្វើការពីមួយថ្ងៃទៅមួយថ្ងៃ ពីមួយអាទិត្យទៅមួយអាទិត្យ

👉 thing /θɪŋ/ (noun) =​ វត្ថុ,របស់
(a device, product, or part of nature that is not named:)
e.g - 👉There’s a new ​ thing that seals plastic bags.
              មាន វត្ថុ/របស់ ថ្មីដែលបិតថង់ផ្លាសស្ទីក
e.g - 👉 There are some nice ​ things in the stores on sale right now.
              មានវត្ថុ/របស់ ល្អមួយចំនួនក្នុងហាងដែលកំពង់ដាក់លក់ឥឡូវនេះ
(used to refer in an approximate way to an idea, subject, event, action, etc.:)
e.g - 👉That was an unkind thing to say. ​
              វាជារឿង ដែលមិនគួរនិយាយ
e.g - 👉 I've got so many things to do I don't know where to start.​
              ខ្ញុំមានការងារ ច្រើនដើម្បីធ្វើ ខ្ញុំមិនដឹងចាប់ផ្តើមពីណាទៅមុនទេ?
e.g - 👉 Your information is correct but you left out one things ​
              ការរៀបរាប់របស់អ្នកត្រូវទាំងអស់ តែអ្នកបែជាភ្លេចរឿងមួយ មួយ

👉 preposition /ˌprep.əˈzɪʃ.ən/ (noun) = ធ្នាក់​ (ជាពាក្យប្រើនៅពីមុខ នាម, ឃ្លានាម ឬ សព្វនាម, ដើម្បីភ្ជាប់ពាក្យ)
(in grammar, a word that is used before a noun, a noun phrase, or a pronoun, connecting it to another word:)
e.g - 👉In the sentences "We jumped in the lake", and "She drove slowly down the track", "in" and "down" are prepositions.
              នៅក្នុងប្រយោគ "We jumped in the lake"​ និង "She drove slowly down the track" "in" និង "down" ជា prepositions

👉 always /ˈɔːl.weɪz/ (adverb) =​ តែងតែ,ជានិច្ចជាកាល
(every time or all the time:)
e.g - 👉It's ​ always cold in this room.
              វា តែងតែត្រជាក់ក្នុងបន្ទប់នេះ
e.g - 👉 She ​ always spells my name wrong.
              នាងតែងតែ ប្រកបឈ្មោះខ្ញុំខុស
always adverb (FOR EVER)
(for ever:)
e.g - 👉I'll always remember you. ​
              ខ្ញុំនឹងចងចាំអ្នករហូត

👉 list /lɪst/ noun =​ បញ្ជី
(a record of short pieces of information, such as people's names, usually written or printed with a single thing on each line and often ordered in a way that makes a particular thing easy to find:)
e.g - 👉Is your name on the list ?
              តើឈ្មោះរបស់អ្នកមាននៅលើ បញ្ជីទេ?
e.g - 👉I've made a list of places I'd like to visit while we're in Paris.
              ខ្ញុំបានបង្កើតបញ្ជីឈ្មោះ កន្លែង ដែលខ្ញុំចង់ទៅលេង កំឡុងពេលពួកយើងនៅប៉ារីស
list verb (MAKE RECORD)
(to make a list, or to include something in a list:)
e.g - 👉I've listed some useful reading material on the handout. ​
              ខ្ញុំបានរាយឈ្មោះ ដែលគេអានច្រើននៅខិត្តប័ណ្ណ

👉 male /meɪl/ adjective =​ ភេទជាប្រុស
(belonging or relating to men:)
e.g - 👉IT is very much a male -dominated industry.
              IT ច្រើនតែជាបុរសដែលធ្វើការត្រួតត្រា

👉 masculine /ˈmæs.kjə.lɪn/ adjective =​ បុរស (ឈ្មោល)
(having characteristics that are traditionally thought to be typical of or suitable for men:)
e.g - 👉She looks a bit masculine in that suit.
              នាងស្លៀកឈុតនឹងទៅស្រដៀងបុរស

👉 gender /ˈdʒen.dər/ noun =​ ភេទ
(the condition of being either male or female:)
e.g - 👉Does this test show the gender of the baby?
              តើការធ្វើតេះនេះ អាចបង្ហាញអោយឃើញពីភេទរបស់ទារកដែរទេ?

👉 female /ˈfiː.meɪl/ adjective =​ ភេទជាស្រី, ស្ត្រី
(belonging or relating to women:)
e.g - 👉She was voted the best female vocalist.
              នាងត្រូវបានគេបោះឆ្នោតជាស្ត្រីអ្នកចំរៀងជើងឯក

👉 feminine /ˈfem.ɪ.nɪn/ adjective =​ ស្រី, ស្ត្រី
(having characteristics that are traditionally thought to be typical of or suitable for a woman:)
e.g - 👉With his long dark eyelashes, he looked almost feminine.
              ជាមួយនឹងរោមភ្នែកពណ៌ខ្មៅវែង គាត់មើលទៅដូចជាមនុស្សស្រី

👉 neuter /ˈnjuːtə/ adjective =​ អភេទ (មិនមែនប្រុស, មិនមែនស្រី ប្រើសម្រាប់វត្ថុ)
GRAMMAR (being a noun or pronoun of a type that refers to things; not masculine or feminine)
e.g - 👉pen, car, clock, mountain, book are neuter.
              pen, car, clock, mountain, book គឺជាneuter

👉 case /keɪs/ nou =​ ករណី
(a particular situation or example of something:)
e.g - 👉Over a hundred people were injured, in several cases seriously.
              មនុស្សជាង100នាក់ បានរងរបួស ក្នុងករណីគ្រូថ្នាក់ធ្ងន់ធ្ងរ
e.g - 👉Jobs are hard to find but in his case that's not the problem because he has so much experience.
              ការងារពិតជាពិបាករកណាស់ តែសម្រាប់ករណីមួយនេះចំពោះគាត់មិនជាបញ្ហានោះទេ ពីព្រោះគាត់មានបទពិសោធន៏ច្រើន
(a large, rectangular container with a handle, for carrying clothes and possessions while travelling:) កេស ឬ វ៉ាលី
e.g - 👉He bought his brother a case of wine for his birthday.
              គាត់បានទិញស្រាមួយកេសជូនបងប្រុសក្នុងថ្ងៃខួបកំណើត
e.g - 👉Will you bring your cases out to the car?
              តើអ្នកនឹងយកវ៉ាលីរបស់អ្នកចេញពីឡានដែលឬទេ?

👉 know /keɪs/ verb =​ ដឹង, ស្គាល់, យល់
(to have information in your mind:)
e.g - 👉"Where did he go?" "I don't know." cases seriously.
              មនុស្សជាង100នាក់ បានរងរបួស ក្នុងករណីគ្រូថ្នាក់ធ្ងន់ធ្ងរ

👉 which /wɪtʃ/ determiner, pronoun = មួយណា
((used in questions and structures in which there is a fixed or limited set of answers or possibilities) what one or ones:)

              ពិធីជប់លៀងមួយមួយណាអ្នកសម្រេចចិត្តទៅ Anna's ឬ Dan's

              ឪពុក និង​ ម្តាយ តើអ្នកស្និទមួយណាជាង

👉 following adjective = បន្តបន្ទាប់, បន្ទាប់

following preposition (AFTER)
e.g - 👉 Following the ballgame, there will be a fireworks display.
               បន្ទាប់ពីបាល់ នឹងមានការបង្ហាញការបាញ់កាំជ្រួច
