              អ្នក ស្តាប់ ដន្ត្រី ប្រភេទអ្វី?

👉 wireless /ˈlɪs.ən/ verb = Radio, ខបករណ៏ភ្ជាប់

e.g - 👉 a wireless connection
               ឧបករណ៏ភ្ជាប់

👉 sometime/ˈsʌm.taɪm/ adverb = ពេលខ្លះ, ជួនកាល, ពេលណាមួយ
(at a time in the future or the past that is not known or not stated:)
e.g - 👉We really should meet sometime soon to discuss the details.
              តាមពិតទៅយើងគួរជួបគ្នា ពេលណាមួយ ឆាប់ៗ ដើម្បីពិភាគ្សាគ្នាអោយលំអិត

👉 cinema/ˈsɪn.ə.mɑː/ noun = រោងកុន
(a theatre where people pay to watch films:)
e.g - 👉The town no longer has a cinema.
              ទីក្រុងឈប់មាន រោងកុន ទៀតហើយ

👉 theatre/ˈθɪə.tər/ noun = ល្ខោន
((the writing or performance of) plays, opera, etc., written to be performed in public:)
e.g - 👉She made her career in the theatre.
              នាងចាប់អាជីពជាអ្នកសម្តែង ល្ខោន។

👉 dinner/ˈdɪn.ər/ noun = អាហារពេលល្ងៀច
(the main meal of the day, usually the meal you eat in the evening but sometimes, in Britain, the meal eaten in the middle of the day:)
e.g - 👉We were just having (our) dinner.
              យើងទើបញាំ អាហារពេលល្ងាច។

👉 supper/ˈsʌp.ər/ noun = អាហារពេលយប់
(a main meal eaten in the evening :)
e.g - 👉Why don't you come to/for supper tonight?
              ហេតុអ្វីអ្នកមិនមក បរិភោគអាហារយប់ យប់នេះ។

👉 generally/ˈdʒen.ə r.əl.i/ adverb = ជាទូទៅ
(usually, or in most situations:)
e.g - 👉The baby generally wakes up three times during the night.
              ទារក ជាទូទៅ ភ្ញាក់បិដង នៅពេលយប់

👉 up /ʌp/ adverb = លើ, ខាងលើ
(towards a higher position; towards a higher value, number, or level:)
e.g - 👉Put those books up on the top shelf.
              ដាក់សៀវភៅទាំងនោះ ខាងលើ ធ្នើ

👉 late /leɪt/ adjective, adverb = យឹត, យូ (ក្បែនិងទីបញ្ចប់នៃពេលវេលាណាមួយ)
late adjective, adverb (NEAR THE END)
((happening or being) near the end of a period of time:)
e.g - 👉We talked late into the night.
              យើងជជែកគ្នាដល់យប់ជ្រៅ។
late adjective, adverb (AFTER EXPECTED TIME) យឺត
e.g - 👉You'll be late for your flight if you don't hurry up.
              អ្នកនឹងយឺតពេល ជិះយន្តហោះ ប្រសិនបើអ្នកមិនប្រញាប់

👉 present /ˈprez.ənt/ noun = កាដូ, ឥឡូវ, បច្ចុប្បន្ន
present noun (SOMETHING GIVEN)
(something that you are given, without asking for it, on a special occasion, especially to show friendship, or to say thank you:)
e.g - 👉a birthday/Christmas/wedding present.
              កាដូ​ birthday/Christmas/wedding ។
present noun (NOW) ឥឡូវ, បច្ចុប្បន្ន
e.g - 👉The play is set in the present.
              កាសម្តែងគឺរៀបចំ ឥឡូវ។

👉 more /mɔːr/ determiner, pronoun, adverb = ថែម, បន្ថែម
(a larger or extra number or amount:)
e.g - 👉Would you like some more food?
              អ្នកត្រូវការអាហារ ថែម​ ទេ?

👉 idiomatic/ˌɪd·i·əˈmæt̬·ɪk/ adjective = ក្រៀមភាសារ
((of a group of words) having a particular meaning that is different from the meanings of each word considered separately:)

👉 ordinary/ˈɔː.dən.əri/ adjective = ធម្មតា
(not different or special or unexpected in any way; usual:)

👉 conversation/ˌkɒn.vəˈseɪ.ʃən/ noun = ការសន្ទា
((a) talk between two or more people in which thoughts, feelings, and ideas are expressed, questions are asked and answered, or news and information is exchanged:)
e.g - 👉She had a strange conversation with the man who moved in upstairs
              នាងមាន ការសន្ទា យ៉ាងចម្លែកមួយបុរសដើរឡើងទៅជាន់លើ

👉 again/əˈɡen/ adverb = ម្តងទៀត
(one more time:)
e.g - 👉Could you spell your name again, please?
              តើអ្នកអាច ប្រកបឈ្មោះ ម្តងទៀត បានទេ?

👉 looking/ˈlʊk.ɪŋ/ adverb =
(having the stated appearance:)
e.g - 👉an odd-looking man
              បុរសដែលមានរូបរាងចម្លែក
e.g - 👉A linen shirt is casual-looking.
              សាច់ក្រណាត់មានលក្ខណះសាមញ្ញ

👉 yellow /ˈjel.əʊ/ adjective = ពណ៌លឿង
(a colour like that of a lemon or gold or the sun:)
e.g - 👉You should wear more yellow - it suits you.
              អ្នកគួរស្លៀកពាក់ ពណ៌លឿង វាសមនឹងអ្នក

👉 corn /kɔːn/ noun = ពោត
((the seeds of) plants, such as wheat, maize, oats, and barley, that can be used to produce flour:)
e.g - 👉grains of corn.
              គ្រាប់ ពោត

👉 behind /bɪˈhaɪnd/ preposition, adverb = ខាងក្រោយ
(at the back (of):)
e.g - 👉Look behind you!
              មើល ខាងក្រោយ អ្នក
e.g - 👉I hung my coat behind the door.
              ខ្ញុំព្យួអាវ នៅ ខាងក្រោយ ទ្វា

👉 dig /dɪɡ/ verb = ជីក
(to break up and move soil using a tool, a machine, or your hands:)
e.g - 👉Digging (in) the garden is good exercise.
              ការចីក ក្នុងសូនច្បារជាលំហាត់ប្រាណដ៏ល្អ

👉 cabbage /ˈkæb.ɪdʒ/ noun = ស្ពៃក្តោប
(a large, round vegetable with large green, white, or purple leaves that can be eaten cooked or uncooked:)
e.g - 👉I like most vegetables but not cabbage.
              ខ្ញុំចូលចិត្តបន្លែទាំងអស់ តែមិនចូលចិត្តស្ពៃក្តោប

👉 potato /pəˈteɪ.təʊ/ noun = ដំឡូង
(a round vegetable that grows underground and has white flesh with light brown, red, or pink skin, or the plant on which these grow:)
e.g - 👉Could you peel the potatoes for me, please?
              តើអ្នកអាចបក ដំឡូង​ អោយខ្ញុំបានទេ?

👉 gate /ɡeɪt/ noun = របង
(a part of a fence or outside wall that is fixed at one side and opens and closes like a door, usually made of metal or wooden strips)
e.g - 👉The lift won't move if the safety gate isn't shut properly.
              ជណ្តើរយន្តមិនដំណើរការទេ ប្រសិនបើ របង​ សុវត្ថិភាពមិនត្រូវបានបិទជិតល្អ

👉 chicken /ˈtʃɪk.ɪn/ noun = មាន់
(a type of bird kept on a farm for its eggs or its meat, or the meat of this bird that is cooked and eaten:)
e.g - 👉A male chicken is called a cock and a female chicken is called a hen.
               មាន់​ ឈ្មោលហៅថា cock និង មាន់ញី ហៅថា hen

👉 bathe /beɪð/ verb = ងូតទឹក
(to swim, especially in the sea, a river, or a lake:)
e.g - 👉Children suffering from the illness had bathed in sea water contaminated by sewage.
              ក្មេងៗ គ្រុនក្តៅបន្ទាប់ពីបាន ងូតទឹក​ សមុទ្រ ដែលមិនល្អ

👉 bath /bɑːθ/ noun = ធុងសម្រាប់ដាក់ទឹកងូតដែលអាចអោយយើងចូលបាន
(a long plastic, metal, or ceramic container that is filled with water so that you can sit or lie in it to wash your whole body)

👉 bath /bɑːθ/ verb = ងូតទឹក, ដុះសម្អាតខ្លួន
(to wash in a bath or to wash someone in a bath:)
e.g - 👉I usually bath the kids in the evening.
              ជាធម្នតា ខ្ញុំ ងូតទឹក​ អោយក្មេងៗ នៅពេលល្ងាច

👉 climb /klaɪm/ verb = ឡើង
(to go up, or to go towards the top of something:)

e.g - 👉The plane climbed quickly to a height of 30,000 feet.
              យន្តហោះហោះ ឡើង​ យ៉ាងឆាប់រហ័ស ដល់កំពស់ 30,000 feet

👉 step /step/ verb = ចុះ, ឈានចុះ
(to move by lifting your foot and putting it down in a different place, or to put your foot on or in something:)

e.g - 👉Be careful not to step in the mud.
              ប្រយ័ត្ន កុំឈានជើងចុះ​ ភក់

👉 pleased /pliːzd/ adjective = រីករាយ
(happy or satisfied:)

e.g - 👉I'm pleased to hear you're feeling better.
              ខ្ញុំសប្បាយចិត្ត​ លឺថាអ្នកប្រសើរឡើង

👉 manly /ˈmæn.li/ adjective = ដែលពេញលក្ខណះជាបុរស
(having the qualities that people think a man should have:)

e.g - 👉My mother used to tell me it wasn't manly for little boys to cry.
              ម្តាយខ្ញុំប្រាប់ថាជាកូនប្រុស​ គឺមិនសម្រក់ទឹកភ្នែកនោះទេ

👉 gay /ɡeɪ/ adjective = ដែលមានចរឹកខ្ទើយ
(sexually or romantically attracted to people of the same gender and not to people of a different gender:)

e.g - 👉My aunt is gay.
              ម្តាយមីងរបស់ខ្ញុំជាខ្ទើយ​

👉 dine /daɪn/ verb = បរិភោគអាហារ (ល្ងាច)
(to eat the main meal of the day, usually in the evening:)

e.g - 👉He once dined with the president of France.
              គាត់បានរួមអាហារល្ងាច​ បានម្តងដែរ ជាមួយប្រធាតិបតីបារាំង​

👉 everywhere/ˈev.ri.weər/ adverb = គ្រប់ទីកន្លែង
(to, at, or in all places or the whole of a place:)

e.g - 👉His children go everywhere with him.
              កូនរបស់គាត់ទៅ គ្រប់ទីកន្លែង​ ជាមួយគាត់​

👉 everyday/ˈev.ri.deɪ/ adjective = រាល់ថ្ងៃ
(ordinary, typical, or usual:)

e.g - 👉Death was an everyday occurrence during the Civil War.
              ការបាត់បង់ជីវិត បានកើតមាន ជារៀងរាល់ថ្ងៃ​ កំឡុងពេលសង្គ្រាម ស៊ីវិល​

👉 pride/praɪd/ noun = មោទនភាព
(a feeling of pleasure and satisfaction that you get because you or people connected with you have done or got something good:)

e.g - 👉She felt a great sense of pride as she watched him accept the award.
              នាងមានអារម្មណ៏ មោទនភាព​ ខ្លាំងណាស់ ពេលមើលគាត់ទទួលបានរង្វាន់​

👉 nobody/ˈnəʊ.bə.di/ pronoun = គ្មានមនុស្ស
(also no one)
(not anyone:)

e.g - 👉I saw nobody all morning.
              គ្មានឃើញអ្នកណាម្នាក់​ សោះពេញមួយព្រឹកនេះ​

👉 nothing/ˈnʌθ.ɪŋ/ pronoun = គ្មានរបស់អ្វី
(not anything:)

e.g - 👉There's nothing in the drawer - I took everything out.
              គ្មានរបស់អ្វី​ នៅក្នុងថតទុកទេ, ខ្ញុំបានយកគ្រប់យ៉ាងចេញអស់ហើយ​

👉 nowhere /ˈnəʊ.weər/ adverb = គ្មានកន្លែង
(in, at, or to no place; not anywhere:)

e.g - 👉These young people have nowhere (else) to go.
              ក្មេងប្រុសទាំងនេះ គ្មានកន្លែង​ (ផ្សេង)​ ត្រូវទៅទេ

👉 none /nʌn/ pronoun = គ្មាន, មិនមាន
(not one (of a group of people or things), or not any:)

e.g - 👉None of my children has/have blonde hair.
              កូនៗរបស់ខ្ញុំគ្មាន​ សក់ពណ៌ទងដែងទេ
e.g - 👉"I'd like some more cheese." "I'm sorry there's none left".
              ខ្ញុំត្រូវការ cheese បន្ថែមទៀត អោយខ្ញុំសូមទោសមិនមាន​ សល់ទេ

👉 somebody /ˈsʌm.bə.di/ pronoun =​អ្នកណាម្នាក់, មនុស្សមួយចំនួយ
(someone)

e.g - 👉Somebody in the office will know.
              មនុស្សមួយចំនួន​ ក្នុងការិយាល័យ នឹងយល់
e.g - 👉Somebody must have seen it happen.
              មានអ្នកណាម្នាក់​ ច្បាស់ជាបានឃើញរឿងរាវកើតឡើង

👉 somewhere /ˈsʌm.weər/ adverb =​ កន្លែងណាមួយ
(in or at a place having a position that is not stated or not known:)

e.g - 👉You must have put their letter somewhere!
              អ្នកត្រូវដាក់សំបុត្រពួកគេនៅកន្លែងណាមួយ​
e.g - 👉Can we go somewhere else to talk - it's very noisy here.
              យើងអាចទៅរកកន្លែងណាមួយ​ ជជែកគ្នាបានទេ វារញេរញ៉ៃណាស់ទីនេះ

👉 anybody /ˈen.iˌbɒd.i/ pronoun =​ នណាម្នាក់
(anyone)

e.g - 👉She's a bitworried about moving to a big city where she won't know anybody.
              នាងមានការព្រួយបារម្ភពីការផ្លាស់ប្តូរទៅរស់ទៅទីក្រុងធំ ជាកន្លែងដែលនាងមិនស្គាល់នណាម្នាក់សោះ​
e.g - 👉I didn't know anybody at the party.
              ខ្ញុំមិនស្គាល់នណាម្នាក់​ សោះនៅកម្មវិធី

👉 anything /ˈen.i.θɪŋ/ pronoun =​ អ្វីមួយ
(used in questions and negatives to mean "something":)

e.g - 👉Is there anything I can do to help?
              មានអ្វីមួយ ដែលខ្ញុំអាចជួយបាន
e.g - 👉Let me know if anything happens, won't you?
              អោយខ្ញុំដឹងប្រសិនមានអ្វីមួយកើតឡើង​ ដែលអ្នកមិនដឹង

👉 anywhere /ˈen.i.θɪŋ/ pronoun =​ កន្លែងណាមួយ, គ្រប់កន្លែង
(in, to, or at any place:)

e.g - 👉I can't find my keys anywhere.
              ខ្ញុំរកមិនឃើញសោគ្រប់កន្លែង
e.g - 👉Is there anywhere to eat around here?
              មានកន្លែងណាមួយដើម្បីបរិភោគទេ នៅជុំវិញទីនេះ

👉 greeting /ˈɡriː.tɪŋ/ noun =​ ជំរាបសួរ,​(គោរព)
(something friendly or polite that you say or do when you meet or welcome someone:)

e.g - 👉He nodded his head in greeting.
              គាត់អោនក្បាលចុះជាការគោរព

👉 good morning /ˌɡʊd ˈmɔː.nɪŋ/ exclamation =​ អរុណសួស្តី (ពេលព្រឹក)
(something you say to greet someone politely when you meet them in the morning)

e.g - 👉 Good morning! How are you?
              អរុណសួស្តី សុខសប្បាយទេ?

👉 good afternoon /ˌɡʊd ˌɑːf.təˈnuːn/ exclamation =​ សួស្តីពេលរសៀល (ពេលរសៀល)
(something you say to greet someone politely when you meet them in the afternoon)

e.g - 👉 Good afternoon! How are you?
              រសៀលសួស្តី សុខសប្បាយទេ?

👉 good evening /ˌɡʊd ˈiːv.nɪŋ/ exclamation =​ ល្ងាចសួស្តី (ពេលល្ងាច)
(something you say to greet someone politely when you meet them in the evening)

e.g - 👉 Good​ evening! How are you?
              ល្ងាចសួស្តី សុខសប្បាយទេ?

👉 England/ˈɪŋ.ɡlənd/ noun =​ ប្រទេសអង់គ្លេស

e.g - 👉Did you have a nice trip?
              តើអ្នកមានដំណើរកម្សាន្តរីករាយទេ?

👉 certainly /ˈsɜː.tən.li/ adverb = តាមពិតទៅ, ជាក់ច្បាស់, ពិតប្រាកដ
(used to reply completely or to emphasize something and show that there is no doubt about it:)

e.g - 👉"This is rather a difficult question." "Yes, it's certainly not easy."
              នេះជាសំនួរមួដែរលំបាក បាទ/ចាស ពិតប្រាកដណាស់វាមិនងាយស្រួលនោះទេ

👉 swimming /ˈswɪm.ɪŋ/ noun = ការហែលទឺក
(the activity or sport of swimming:)

e.g - 👉The doctor recommended swimming as the best all-round exercise.
              គ្រូវពេទ្យនិយាយថា ការហែលទឺកជាលំហាត់ប្រាណដែលល្អ

👉 polite /pəˈlaɪt/ adjective = គួរសម
(behaving in a way that is socially correct and shows understanding of and care for other people's feelings:)

e.g - 👉He was too polite to point out my mistake.
              គាត់បានចង្អុលបង្ហាញរាល់កំហុលរបស់ ដោយការ គួរសម

👉 sleep /sliːp/ noun = ដេក
(the resting state in which the body is not active and the mind is unconscious:)

e.g - 👉I must get some sleep - I'm exhausted.
              ខ្ញុំត្រូវការដេកបន្តិ ខ្ញុំអស់កំលាំង

👉 eater /ˈiː.tər/ noun = អ្នកញាំ
(someone who eats a particular amount or type of food, eats in a particular way, or has a particular attitude towards food:)

e.g - 👉I think he was the champion eater of the world.
              ខ្ញុំគិតថាគាត់ជាអ្នកញាំជើងឯកពិភពលោក

👉 sleeper /ˈsliː.pər/ noun = អ្នកដេក
(someone who sleeps in the stated way:)

e.g - 👉I'm a light sleeper - the slightest noise wakes me.
              ខ្ញុំជាអ្នកដេកឆាប់ភ្ញាក់(រវៀស) លឺសំលេងតែបន្តិចក៏ភ្ញាក់ដែរ

👉 good-hearted/ˌɡʊdˈhɑː.tɪd/ adjective = ចិត្តល្អ, សប្បុរស
(kind and generous)

e.g - 👉He's a good-hearted kid who loves to help out.
              គាត់ជាក្មេងម្នាក់ដែលចិត្តល្អចូលចិត្តជួយគេ

👉 follow /ˈfɒl.əʊ/ verb = តាម, ដើរតាម
(to move behind someone or something and go where he, she, or it goes:)

e.g - 👉A dog followed us home.
              ឆ្កែដើរតាមយើងទៅផ្ទះ

👉 meet /miːt/ verb = ជួប
(to see and talk to someone for the first time:)

e.g - 👉Would you like to meet my sister?
              តើអ្នកចង់ជួបប្អូនស្រីខ្ញុំរឺ?

shelves Plural of shelf

👉 shelf /ʃelf/ noun = ធ្នើ
(a long, flat board fixed horizontally, usually against a wall or inside a cupboard so that objects can be stored on it:)

e.g - 👉One wall had shelves from floor to ceiling, crammed with books.
              នៅជាប់ជញ្ជាំងមានធ្នើ ពីក្រោមដល់ទល់ពិដាន ដែផ្ទុកទៅដោយសៀវភៅជាច្រើន

👉 prefix /ˈpriː.fɪks/ noun = បុព្វបទ
(a letter or group of letters added to the beginning of a word to make a new word:)

e.g - 👉In the word "unimportant", "un-" is a prefix.
              ក្នុងពាក្យ "unimportant",​ "un-" ជាបុព្វបទ

👉 Parisian /pəˈrɪz.i.ən/ adjective = ប៉ារីស
(from, belonging to, or relating to the city of Paris in France:)

e.g - 👉She's got that Parisian chic.
              នាងមានម៉ូដតាមបែបប៉ារីស

👉 unhappy /ʌnˈhæp.i/ adjective = មិនរីករាយ
(sad or not satisfied:)

e.g - 👉That's enough to make anyone unhappy.
              ល្មមហើយដែលធ្វើអោយគេមិនសប្បាយចិត្ត

👉 unhealthy /ʌnˈhel.θi/ adjective = សុខភាពមិនល្អ
(not good for your health:)

e.g - 👉an unhealthy diet
              របបអាហារមិនចម្រើនដល់សុខភាព

👉 uncommon /ʌnˈhel.θi/ adjective = មិនធម្មតា
(not good for your health:)

e.g - 👉Accidents due to failure of safety equipment are uncommon nowadays.
              គ្រោះថ្នាក់ ដោយហេតុតែ ឧបករណ៏សុវត្ថិភាពបរាជ័យ គឹមិនត្រូវបានអោយប្រើទេ សព្វថ្ងៃនេះ
e.g - 👉It's not uncommon for people to become ill when they travel.
              វាតែងតែកើតឡើងជាធម្មតា ពេលដែលពួកគេធ្វើដំណើតហើយមានជំងឺ

👉 unpleasant /ʌnˈplez.ənt/ adjective = មិនរីករាយ
(not enjoyable or pleasant:)

e.g - 👉an unpleasant surprise
              ករភ្ញាក់ផ្អើលដែលមិនរំភើប

👉 unlike /ʌnˈlaɪk/ adjective = មិនដូច
(different from:)

e.g - 👉Unlike you, I’m not a great dancer.
              ខ្ញុំមិនពូកែរាំមិនដូច អ្នក

👉 correct /kəˈrekt/ adjective = ត្រឹមត្រូវ
(in agreement with the true facts or with what is generally accepted:)

e.g - 👉a correct answer
              ចម្លើយត្រឹមត្រូវ

👉 incorrect /ˌɪn.kərˈekt/ adjective = មិនត្រឹមត្រូវ
(not correct or not true:)

e.g - 👉a incorrect answer
              ចម្លើយមិនត្រឹមត្រូវ

👉 impolite /ˌɪm.pəlˈaɪt/ adjective = មិនចេះគួរសម
(behaving in a way that is not socially correct and shows a lack of understanding of and care for other people's feelings:)

e.g - 👉It is impolite to point at people.
              វាមិនគួរសមទេកាចង្អុលទៅអ្នកណាម្នាក់

👉 undress /ʌnˈdres/ verb = ដោះសំលៀកបំពាក់
(to remove your clothes or remove the clothes from someone else:)

e.g - 👉Could you undress the kids for bed, Steve?
              តើអ្នកអាយដោះសំលៀកបំពាក់អោយកូនគេងបានទេ?

👉 related /rɪˈleɪ.tɪd/ adjective = ដែលមានទំនាក់ទំនង
(connected:)

e.g - 👉We discussed unemployment and related issues.
              យើងបានពិភាគសារពីបញ្ហាអត់ការងារធ្វើ និង រឿងរាងដែលទាក់ទង

👉 live /lɪv/ verb = រស់នៅ
((to continue) to be alive or have life:)

e.g - 👉[ + to infinitive ] I hope I live to see my grandchildren.
              ខ្ញុំសង្ឃឹមថាខ្ញុំអាចរស់នៅបន្តទៀត ដេម្បីបានឃើញចៅខ្ញុំ

👉 alive /əˈlaɪv/ adjective = មានជិវិត
(living, not dead:)

e.g - 👉He must be 90 if he's still alive.
              គាត់នឹងមានអាយុ 90 ប្រសិនបេគាត់នៅមានជីវិត

👉 rabbit /ˈræb.ɪt/ noun= ទន្សាយ
(a small animal with long ears and large front teeth that moves by jumping on its long back legs, or the meat of this animal eaten as food:)

e.g - 👉a pet rabbit
              សត្វទន្សាយដែលចិញ្ចឹម

👉 dead /ded/ noun= មរណះ,ស្លាប់, ងាប់
(not now living:)

e.g - 👉She's been dead for 20 years now.
              គាត់បានស្លាប់អស់រយះពេល 20ឆ្នាំហើយ

👉 enjoy/ɪnˈdʒɔɪ/ verb= រីករាយ (ពីអ្វីមួយ)
(to get pleasure from something:)

e.g - 👉I really enjoyed that movie/book/concert/party/meal.
              ខ្ញុំពិតជារីករាយthat movie/book/concert/party/meal.

👉 enjoyment/ɪnˈdʒɔɪ.mənt/ noun= ភាពរីករាយ (ពីអ្វីមួយ)
(the feeling of enjoying something:)

e.g - 👉Knowing the ending already didn't spoil my enjoyment of the movie.
              ការដឹងពីទីបញ្ចប់នៃសាច់រៀង វាមិនបានធ្វើអោយខ្ញុំមានភាពរីករាយនោះទេ

👉 sorry/ˈsɒr.i/ adjective = សុំទោស, សោកស្តាយ
(feeling sadness, sympathy, or disappointment, especially because something unpleasant has happened or been done:)

e.g - 👉I'm just sorry about all the trouble I've caused her
              ខ្ញុំទើបតែសុំទោស អំពីរឿងរាងគ្រប់យ៉ាងដែលខ្ញុំបានបង្កទៅលើនាង

👉 sorrowful/ˈsɒr.əʊ.fəl/ adjective = ទុក្ខព្រួយខ្លាំង
(very sad:)

e.g - 👉With a sorrowful sigh she folded the letter and put it away.
              ជាមួយនិងការដកដង្ហើម ដោយក្តីទុក្ខព្រួយ នាងបានបទសំបុត្រហើយដាក់វាទីឆ្ងាយ

👉 certain/ˈsɜː.tən/ adjective = ដែលប្រាកដ
(having no doubt or knowing exactly that something is true, or known to be true, correct, exact, or effective:)

e.g - 👉[ + (that) ] Are you absolutely certain (that) you gave them the right number?
              តើអ្នកប្រាកដ ថាអ្នកអោយលេខត្រឹមត្រូវទៅគាត់

👉 uncertain/ʌnˈsɜː.tən/ adjective= មិនប្រាកដ
(not knowing what to do or believe, or not able to decide about something:)

e.g - 👉[ + question word ] She's uncertain whether to go to New Zealand or not.
              នាងមិនប្រាកដទេថា ត្រូវទៅឬអត់

👉 politely/pəˈlaɪt.li/ adv = យ៉ាងគួរសម
(in a polite way:)

e.g - 👉He told them politely to leave him in peace.
              គាត់ប្រាប់ពួគគេយ៉ាងគួរសម អោយចាកចេញពីគាត់ដោយសន្តិភាព

👉 politeness /pəˈlaɪt.nəs/ noun = ភាពគួរសម
(behaviour that is socially correct and shows understanding of and care for other people's feelings:)

e.g - 👉She smiled at the boy's politeness.
              គាត់ញញឹមដាក់ក្មេងប្រុសដែលចេះគួរសម

👉 tense /tens/ noun = កាល
(any of the forms of a verb which show the time at which an action happened:)

e.g - 👉"I sing" is in the present tense​ and "I sang" is in the past tense.
              "I sing" នៅក្នុង បច្ចុប្បន្នកាល​​ និង "I sang" នៅក្នុងអតីតកាល

👉 e.g./iːˈdʒiː/ = for example (ជាឧទាហរណ៏)
(also eg)
(exempli gratia: a Latin phrase that means "for example". It can be pronounced as "e.g." or "for example":)

e.g - 👉You should eat more food that contains a lot of fibre, e.g. fruit, vegetables, and bread.
              អ្នកគួរញាំអាហារដែលមានផ្ទុក fiber ច្រើនបន្ថែមទៀតឧទាហរណ៏​​ ដូចជា ផ្លែឈើ, បន្លែ, និង​ នំបុ័ង្គ

👉 place/pleɪs/ noun = ទីកន្លែង
(an area, town, building, etc.:)

e.g - 👉Her garden was a cool pleasant place to sit.
              សួនច្បារ របស់នាង មានកន្លែង​​ អង្គុយត្រជាក់ស្រួល

take place (ជំនួសកន្លែង)
(to happen:)
e.g - 👉The handover to the new owners will take place in July.
              អ្នកកាន់ការថ្មី នឹងមកនឹងមកជំនួសកន្លែង​​ ក្នុងខែកក្តា

👉 possessive /pəˈzes.ɪv/ adjective = កម្មសិទ្ឋិ
(If you are possessive about something that you own, you do not like lending it to other people or sharing it with other people:)

e.g - 👉He's pretty possessive about his iPod - I wouldn't dare ask to borrow it.
              គាត់មានការហួងហែង​​ អំពី ipod កាត់ខ្លាំងណាស់ ខ្ញុំមិនហានខ្ចីទេ

👉 adjective /ˈædʒ.ek.tɪv/ noun = គុណនាម
(a word that describes a noun or pronoun:)

e.g - 👉"Big", "boring", "purple", and "obvious" are all adjectives.
              "Big", "boring", "purple", and "obvious" ទាំងអស់នេះជាគុណនាម

👉 fun /fʌn/ noun = សប្បាយ
(pleasure, enjoyment, or entertainment:)

e.g - 👉Have fun (= enjoy yourself)!
              រីករាយ ជាមួយខ្លួនឯង

👉 funny /ˈfʌn.i/ adjective = កំប្លែង
(humorous; causing laughter:)

e.g - 👉Do you know any funny jokes?
              ​ តើអ្នកមានចេះរឿងកំប្លែង ខ្លះទេ?

👉 express /ɪkˈspres/ adjective = បង្ហាញ (អារម្មណ៏,គំនិង,ហេតុការណ៏)
(to show a feeling, opinion, or fact:)

e.g - 👉Her eyes expressed deep sadness.
              ​ ភ្នែករបស់នាងបានបង្ហាញ នៅភាពទុក្ខសោកយ៉ាងខ្លាំង

👉 ago/əˈɡəʊ/ adverb= កន្លងផុតទៅ
(back in time from the present:)

e.g - 👉He left the house over an hour ago
              ​ គាត់បានចេញពីផ្ទះប៉ុន្មានម៉ោងកន្លងទៅហើយ

👉 regular/ˈreɡ.jə.lər/ adjective = ទៀងទាត់​, ជាប្រចាំ
(happening or doing something often:)

e.g - 👉She goes to her doctor for regular check-ups.
              ​ នាងទៅជួបគ្រូពេទ្យដើម្បីពិនិត្យសុខភាពជាប្រចាំ

👉 bucket/ˈbʌk.ɪt/ noun = ធុង​(សម្រាប់ដាក់ទឹក)
(a container with an open top and a handle, often used for carrying liquids:)

e.g - 👉Armed with a bucket and a mop, I started washing the floor.
              ​ ដៃយួរធុងទឹក និងក្រាណាត់ជូត ចាប់ផ្តើមសម្អាតកម្រាល

👉 never/ˈnev.ər/ adverb = មិនដែល, មិនធ្លាប់
(not at any time or not on any occasion:)

e.g - 👉We've never been to Australia.
              ​ ពួកយើងមិនដែរ ទៅដល់ Australia ទេ

👉 heart/hɑːt/ noun = បេះដូង
(the organ in your chest that sends the blood around your body:)

e.g - 👉he is a gook hearted.
              ​ គាត់ជាមនុស្សដែលមានបេះដូង ចិត្តល្អ

👉 description/dɪˈskrɪp.ʃən/ noun = ការពិពណ៌នា
(something that tells you what something or someone is like:)

e.g - 👉Write a description of your favourite beach.
              ​ សរសេរពិពណ៌នា ពីឆ្នេរដែលអ្នកពេញចិត្ត

👉 comparison/kəmˈpær.ɪ.sən/ noun = ការប្រៀបធៀប
(the act of comparing two or more people or things:)

e.g - 👉They made a comparison of different countries' eating habits.
              ​ ពួកគេបានធ្វើការប្រៀបធៀប ពីទំលាប់បរិបភោគនៃប្រទេសផ្សេងៗគ្នា

👉 scene /siːn/ noun = ឈុត ឆាក (សម្តែង)
(a part of a play or film in which the action stays in one place for a continuous period of time:)

e.g - 👉It took seven retakes to get the scene exactly right.
              ​ វាត្រូវបានចំណាយពេលអស់7លើក ដើម្បីសម្រេចបានឈុត ដ៏ត្រឹមត្រូវមួយ

👉 had /hæd/ verb = មាន
had verb (HAVE) (past simple and past participle of have , also used with the past participle of other verbs to form the past perfect:)

e.g - 👉When I was a child I had a dog.
              ​ ពេលខ្ញុំនៅក្មេង ខ្ញុំមាន ឆ្កែមួយ

👉 coming/ˈkʌm.ɪŋ/ adjective = ដែមកដល់ឆាប់ៗ
(happening soon:)

e.g - 👉We look forward to greater success in the coming year.
              ​ យើងរង់ចាំមើលភាពជោគជ័យធំធេងមួយ នៅដាច់ ឆ្នាំនេះ

👉 stead /sted/ noun = ការជំនូស
(in place of someone:)

e.g - 👉The marketing manager was ill and her deputy ran the meeting in her stead.
              ​ អ្នកគ្រប់គ្រងទីផ្សារ បានមានជំងឺ និង អនុប្រធានបានចូលប្រជុំ ជំនូស

👉 long/lɒŋ/ adjective = វែង, ពេលវែង,​ យូ
(continuing for a large amount of time:)

e.g - 👉I've been waiting a long time.
              ខ្ញុំបានរងចាំ យូមកហើយ

👉 stay/steɪ/ verb = នៅ
(to not move away from or leave a place or situation:)

e.g - 👉Stay until the rain has stopped.
              នៅរហូតដល់ឈប់ភ្លៀង

👉 fortnight /ˈfɔːt.naɪt/ noun = ពីរសប្តាហ៏
(a period of two weeks:)

e.g - 👉How much would it cost to hire a car for a fortnight?
              ជួលឡានពីរសប្តាហ៏តំលៃបុន្មាន?

👉 busy /ˈbɪz.i/ adjective = រវល់
(If you are busy, you are working hard, or giving your attention to a particular thing:)

e.g - 👉Mum was busy in the kitchen.
              ម្តាយជាប់រវល់ក្នុងផ្ទះបាយ

👉 sure /ʃɔːr/ adjective = ប្រាកដ, ច្បាស់
(certain; without any doubt:)

e.g - 👉I'm sure (that) I left my keys on the table.
              ខ្ញុំច្បាស់ណាស់ថាខ្ញុំបានទុកសោនៅលើតុ

👉 neither/ˈnaɪ.ðər/ /ˈniː.ðər/ determiner, pronoun, conjunction, adverb = មិនទាំងអស់
(not either of two things or people:)

e.g - 👉Neither of my parents likes my boyfriend.
              ទាំងម្តាយទាំងឪពុកមិនពេញចិត្តមិត្តប្រុសខ្ញុំទេ

neither ... nor
(used when you want to say that two or more things are not true:)
e.g - 👉Neither my mother nor my father went to university.
              ទាំងម្តាយទាំងឪពុកមិនបានចូលរៀន សកលទេ

👉 either/ˈaɪ.ðər/ /ˈiː.ðər/ adverb = បានទាំងអស់​ (អាចប្រើក្នុងទម្រង់ បដិសេធ ជំនួសអោយពក្យផងដែរ, ដែរ ("also, too"))
(used in negative sentences instead of "also" or "too":)

e.g - 👉I don't eat meat and my husband doesn't either.
              ខ្ញុំមិនបរិភោគសាច់ទេ ហើយ ប្តីខ្ញុំក៏មិនបិរិភោគដែរ

either ... or
(used when referring to a choice between two possibilities:)
e.g - 👉We can either eat now or after the show - it's up to you.
              យើងអាចញាំឥឡូវបានឬបន្ទាប់ពីការសម្តែងចប់ សម្រេចលើអ្នក

👉 lucky /ˈlʌk.i/ adjective = សំណាង
(having good things happen to you by chance:)

e.g - 👉He's lucky that he wasn't fired.
              គាត់មានសំណាង​ ដែលមិនត្រូវបានភ្លើងឆេះ

👉 than /ðæn/ preposition, conjunction = (ប្រើសម្រាប់ក្នុងន័យប្រៀងធៀប របស់ពីរយ៉ាង)
(used to join two parts of a comparison:)

e.g - 👉My son is a lot taller than my daughter.
              កូនប្រុសខ្ញុំទាំងអស់ ខ្ពស់ជាង​ កូនស្រី

👉 family /ˈfæm.əl.i/ noun = គ្រួសារ
(a group of people who are related to each other, such as a mother, a father, and their children:)

e.g - 👉He doesn't have any family.
              គាត់គ្មានគ្រូសារទេ

👉 quite /kwaɪt/ adverb = ណាស់, ទាំងស្រុង
(completely:)

e.g - 👉The two situations are quite different.
              ស្ថានភាពទាំងពីរនេះគឺខុសគ្នាទាំងស្រុង

👉 remind /rɪˈmaɪnd/ verb = នឹកឃើញឡើងវិញ, រលឹកឡើងវិញុ, រលឹកនណាម្នាក់
(to make someone think of something they have forgotten or might have forgotten:)

e.g - 👉Could you remind Paul about dinner on Saturday?
              អ្នកអាចជួយរលឹក Paul អំពីរការញាំអាហារល្ងាចនៅថ្ងៃសៅរ៏ផង

👉 young /jʌŋ/ adjective = ក្មេង
(having lived or existed for only a short time and not old:)

e.g - 👉His girlfriend's very young.
              មិត្តស្រីគាត់ក្មេង ណាស់

👉 twin /twɪn/ noun = កូនភ្លោះ
(either of two children born to the same mother on the same occasion:)

e.g - 👉My sister has twin sons.
              បងស្រីខ្ញុំមានកូនភ្លោះ ប្រុស

👉 exact/ɪɡˈzækt/ adjective = ប្រាកដ
(in great detail, or complete, correct, or true in every way:)

e.g - 👉The exact distance is 1.838 metres.
              ចម្ងាយប្រាកដ គឺ​ 1.838​ម៉ែត្រ

👉 fair/feər/ adjective = ស្មើរភាពគ្នា, យុត្តិធម៌
(treating someone in a way that is right or reasonable, or treating a group of people equally and not allowing personal opinions to influence your judgment:)

e.g - 👉Why should I have to do all the cleaning? It's not fair!
              ហេតុអ្វី ខ្ញុំត្រូវសំអាតទាំងអស់តែម្នាក់ឯង វាមិនស្មើរភាពគ្នាទេ

fair adjective (PALE) ស្លេក
((of skin) pale, or (of hair) pale yellow or gold:)
e.g - 👉She's got fair hair and blue eyes.
              នាងមានសក់ ស្លេក និង ភ្នែកពណ៏ខៀវ

👉 fat/fæt/ adjective = ធាត់
(having a lot of flesh on the body:)

e.g - 👉He eats all the time but he never gets fat.
              គាត់បរិភោគ គ្រប់ពេល តែគាត់មិនធាត់ សោះ

👉 thin/fæt/ adjective = ស្តើង, ស្គម
(Not Thick, Not fat)

e.g - 👉a thin book.
              សៀវភៅស្តើង

e.g - 👉the thin man.
              បុរសស្គម

👉 suppose/səˈpəʊz/ verb = ជឿរថា
(to think that something is likely to be true:)

e.g - 👉Dan didn't answer his phone, so I suppose (that) he's busy.
              dan មិនបានឆ្លើយតប ទូរស័ព្ទទេ ដូច្នេះខ្ញុំជឿរថា គាត់រវល់

👉 home/həʊm/ adverb = ផ្ទះ
(at or to your house or the place where you live:)

e.g - 👉She decided to give up and go home.
              នាងសម្រេចចិត្តថា បញ្ឈប់ត្រឹមនឹង ហើយទៅផ្ទះ

👉 noisy /ˈnɔɪ.zi/ adjective = ឡូឡា
(making a lot of noise:)

e.g - 👉noisy neighbours
              អ្នកជិតខាងឡូឡា

👉 expect /ɪkˈspekt/ verb = រំពឹងទុក
(to think or believe something will happen, or someone will arrive:)

e.g - 👉 We are expecting a lot of applicants for the job.
              យើងរំពឹងថា នឹងមានការដាក់ពាក្យស្នើការងារច្រើន

👉 fight /faɪt/ verb = វាយតប់
(to use physical force to try to defeat another person or group of people:)

e.g - 👉There were children fighting in the playground.
              មានក្មេងៗ បានវាយតប់ គ្នា នៅកន្លែងលេង

👉 remember /rɪˈmem.bər/ verb = ចង់ចាំ
( to be able to bring back a piece of information into your mind, or to keep a piece of information in your memory:)

e.g - 👉"Where did you park the car?" "I can't remember."
              តើអ្នកចតឡាននៅកន្លែងណា ខ្ញុំមិនបានចងចាំ ទេ

👉 uncle/ˈʌŋ.kəl/ noun = អ៊ំ, ពូ
( the brother of someone's mother or father, or the husband of someone's aunt or uncle:)

e.g - 👉I have lots of uncles and aunts.
              ខ្ញំុមានអ៊ំប្រុស និងអ៊ំស្រី ច្រើនណាស់

👉 advise/ədˈvaɪz/ noun = ដំបូមាន, នែនាំ, ផ្តល់យោបល់
(to give someone advice:)

e.g - 👉His doctor advised him against smoking.
              គ្រូពេទ្យគាត់ បាននែនាំ អោយគាត់ឈប់ជក់បារី

👉 hundred/ˈhʌn.drəd/ number = មួយរយ (១០០)
(the number 100:)

e.g - 👉That dress costs hundreds of dollars.
              សំលៀកបំពាក់នេះ តំលៃ១០០ ដុល្លា

👉 hit /hɪt/ verb = ដាល់, វាយ
(to move your hand or an object onto the surface of something so that it touches it, usually with force:)

e.g - 👉Teachers are not allowed to hit their pupils.
              គ្រូមិនអនុញ្ញាតអោយវាយ សិស្សទេ

👉 thousand /ˈθaʊ.zənd/ number = មួយពាន់ (១០០០)
(the number 1,000:)

e.g - 👉The damage will cost thousands of dollars to repair.
              ការខូចខាត នឹងត្រូវចំណាយថ្លៃ អស់១០០០ ដុល្លាដើម្បីជួសជុលឡើងវិញ

👉 degree /dɪˈɡriː/ noun = កម្រិត
((an) amount or level of something:)

e.g - 👉This job demands a high degree of skill.
              ការងារនេះ ទាមទារ ជំនាញកម្រិត ខ្ពស់

((written abbreviation deg.) any of various units of measurement, especially of temperature or angles, usually shown by the symbol ° written after a number:)​ ដឺក្រេ

e.g - 👉a difference of three degrees.
              ខុសគ្នាបីដឺក្រេ.

(a course of study at a college or university, or the qualification given to a student after he or she has completed his or her studies:)​ សញ្ញាប័ត្រ

e.g - 👉She has a bachelor's degree.
              នាងមានសញ្ញាប័ត្របរិញ្ញា.

👉 positive /ˈpɒz.ə.tɪv/ adjective = វិជ្ជមាន
(full of hope and confidence, or giving cause for hope and confidence:)

e.g - 👉There was a very positive response to our new design - people seemed very pleased with it.
              បានមានការឆ្លើយតប្រកបដោយភាពវិជ្ជមាន មកកាន់ការរចនាថ្មីរបស់យើង មនុស្សហាក់រីករាយណាស់ជាមួយវា

( certain and without any doubt:) ច្បាស់លាស់, ប្រាកដជា

e.g - 👉"It was him - I saw him take it." "Are you positive about that?"
              "គឺគាត់ហ្នឹងហើយ - ខ្ញុំបានឃើញគាត់យក" "តើអ្នក ច្បាស់ហើយ ថាគាត់ជាអ្នកយក?"

👉 call /kɔːl/ verb = ហៅ
(to give someone or something a name, or to know or address someone by a particular name:)

e.g - 👉They've called the twins Edward and Thomas.
              ពួកគេបានហៅ កូនភ្លោះថា Edward និង Thomas

👉 comparative /kəmˈpær.ə.tɪv/ noun = ប្រៀបធៀប
(the form of an adjective or adverb that expresses a difference in amount, number, degree, or quality:)

e.g - 👉"Fatter" is the comparative of "fat".


👉 add /æd/ verb = បញ្ចូល, បន្ថែម
(to put two or more numbers or amounts together to get a total:)

e.g - 👉Beat the butter and sugar together and slowly add the eggs.
              សាច់ បឺ​ និងស្ករ ជាមួយគ្នា ហើយបន្ថែម ស៊ុតយឺតៗ

👉 end /end/ noun = ចុងបញ្ចប់
(the part of a place or thing that is furthest away from the centre:)

e.g - 👉We damaged the end of the piano when we moved it.
              យើងបានធ្វើអោយបែកផ្នែកខាងចុង នៃ ព្យាណូ នៅពេលដែលយើងរំកិលវា

👉 single /ˈsɪŋ.ɡəl/ adjective = តែមួយ
(one only:)

e.g - 👉Not a single person offered to help her.
              មិនមែនមនុស្សតែម្នាក់ ទេដែលត្រូវបានអោយទៅជួយនាង

(not married, or not having a romantic relationship with someone:) នៅលីវ ឬនៅកំលោះ

e.g - 👉He's been single for so long now, I don't think he'll ever marry.
              គាត់នៅកំលោះអស់រយះពេលយូរមកហើយ ដល់ឥឡូវ ខ្ញុំមិនគិតទេថាគាត់រៀបការ

👉 double /ˈdʌb.əl/ adjective = ទ្វេរដង
( twice the size, amount, price, etc., or consisting of two similar things together:)

e.g - 👉The word "cool" has a double "o" in the middle.
              ពាក្យ "cool" មាន "o"ពីរដង នៅកណ្តាល

👉 superlative /suːˈpɜː.lə.tɪv/ noun = អស្ចារ្យ
(the form of an adjective or adverb that expresses that the thing or person being described has more of the particular quality than anything or anyone else of the same type:)

e.g - 👉"Richest" is the superlative of "rich".
              

(of the highest quality; the best:) e.g - 👉We went to a superlative restaurant.
              ​ យើងទៅកាន់ ភោជនីដ្ឋានដែលអស្ចារ្យ

👉 particular /pəˈtɪk.jə.lər/ adjective = ពិសេស
(special, or this and not any other:)

e.g - 👉"Why did you ask?" "Oh, no particular reason, just making conversation."
              ​ "ហេតុអ្វីបានអ្នកសូរ?" "អូ គ្មានហេតុផលពិសេសអីទេ គ្រាត់តែចង់និយាយគ្នាលេងធម្មតា

👉 gerund/ˈdʒer.ənd/ noun
(a word ending in "-ing" that is made from a verb and used like a noun:)

e.g - 👉In the sentence "Everyone enjoyed Tyler's singing", the word "singing" is a gerund.
              ​

👉 verbal/ˈvɜː.bəl/ adjective = ជាការនិយាយ
(spoken rather than written:)

e.g - 👉Do you have it down in writing, or was it just a verbal agreement?
              តើអ្នកមានការសរសេរជាអក្សរ ឬគ្រាន់តែជាកិច្ចព្រមព្រៀង​ ផ្ទាល់មាត់

👉 camp /kæmp/ noun = តង់ ឬជំរុំ (verb) បោះតង់
(to put up a tent and stay in it for a short while, for example while on holiday:)

e.g - 👉We camped on one of the lower slopes of the mountain.
              យើង​ បោះតង់នៅជំរេលភ្នំមួយ

👉 indirect /In daɪˈrekt/ adjective = មិនផ្ទាល់, ដោយប្រយោល

👉 direct /daɪˈrekt/ adjective = ផ្ទាល់, តម្រង់ទៅកាន់
(going in a straight line towards somewhere or someone without stopping or changing direction:)

e.g - 👉She decided to take direct control of the project.
              នាងសម្រេចចិត្តត្រួតពិនិត្យកម្រោងនេះ​ ផ្ទាល់

👉 priority /praɪˈɒr.ə.ti/ noun = អាទិភាព, ជាចម្បង
(something that is very important and must be dealt with before other things:)

e.g - 👉My first/top priority is to find somewhere to live.
              ​ អាទិភាពចម្បងរបស់ខ្ញុំ គឺស្វែងរកកន្លែងណាមួយដើម្បីរស់នៅ

👉 beside/bɪˈsaɪd/ preposition = នៅគៀន, នៅក្បែ
(at the side of, next to:)

e.g - 👉Come and sit here beside me.
              ​ ចូលមកអង្គុយក្បែខ្ញុំ

👉 modify /ˈmɒd.ɪ.faɪ/ verb = កែប្រែ
(to change something such as a plan, opinion, law, or way of behaviour slightly, usually to improve it or make it more acceptable:)

e.g - 👉The school board decided to modify its existing employment policy.
              ​គ្រុមព្រឹក្សាសាលាបានធ្វើការសម្រេចចិត្ត កែប្រែរាល់គោលនយោបាយដែលមានស្រាប់របស់ខ្លួន

👉 confuse /kənˈfjuːz/ verb = ច្រឡំ
(to mix up someone's mind or ideas, or to make something difficult to understand:)

e.g - 👉You're confusing me with my sister - she's the singer.
              ​អ្នកកំពង់ ច្រឡំជាមួយប្អូនស្រីហើយ​ - គាត់ជាអ្នកចំរៀង

👉 composition/ˌkɒm.pəˈzɪʃ.ən/ noun = ការតាក់តែនិពន្ឋ
(something that a person has created or written, esp. a text, a work of art, or a piece of music, or the act of creating or writing something:)

e.g - 👉a composition for piano and flute,
              ​ការតាក់តែនិពន្ឋបទភ្លេងសម្រាប់ព្យាណូ និងខ្លុយ

👉 general/ˈdʒen.ər.əl/ adjective = ទូទៅ
(involving or relating to most or all people, things, or places, especially when these are considered as a unit:)

e.g - 👉There is general concern about rising crime rates.
               មានការផ្តោតជា​ទូទៅអំពីការកើតឡើងឧក្រឹដ្ឋកម្ម

👉 part /pɑːt/ noun = ផ្នែក
(some but not all of a thing:)

e.g - 👉Part of my steak isn't cooked properly.
               ផ្នែកមួយរបស់ steak មិនឆ្អិនល្អទេ

👉 idea/aɪˈdɪə/ noun = គំនិត, ការគិត
(a suggestion or plan for doing something:)

e.g - 👉That's a good idea!
              មាន គំនិតល្អ

👉 least/liːst/ adverb, determiner, pronoun = យ៉ាងហោចណាស់
(less than anything or anyone else; the smallest amount or number:)

e.g - 👉I like the green one least of all.
              ខ្ញុំចូលចិត្តពណ៌បៃតងយ៉ាងហោយមួយក្នុងចំណោមទាំងអស់

👉 youth/juːθ/ noun = វ័យក្មេង
(the period of your life when you are young, or the state of being young:)

e.g - 👉I was a fairly good football player in my youth.
              ខ្ញុំពូកែបាល់ទាត់កាលនៅវ័យក្មេង

👉 bus/bʌs/ noun = ឡានក្រុង
(a large vehicle in which people are driven from one place to another:)

e.g - 👉You should take the bus/go by bus (= travel by bus) if you want to see the sights.
              អ្នកអាធ្វើដំណើរតាមរថយន្តក្រុង ប្រសិនអ្នកចង់ឃើញទេសភាព

👉 taxi/ˈtæk.si/ noun = រថយន្តឈ្នួល
(a car with a driver who you pay to take you somewhere:)

e.g - 👉I took a taxi from the station to the hotel.
              ជិះឡានឈ្នួល ពីស្ថានីយ៏ទៅសណ្ឋាគារ

👉 library /ˈlaɪ.brər.i/ noun = បណ្ណាគារ
(a building, room, or organization that has a collection of books, documents, music, and sometimes things such as tools or artwork, for people to borrow, usually without payment:)

e.g - 👉Some libraries were lending MP3 players to students.
              បណ្ណាគារ មួយចំនួនអោយសិស្សខ្ចីជា MP3

👉 museum /mjuːˈziː.əm/ noun = សារៈមន្ទី
(a building where objects of historical, scientific, or artistic interest are kept:)

e.g - 👉the Natural History Museum.
              សារៈមន្ទីប្រវត្តសាស្ត្រ

👉 continuous/kənˈtɪn.ju.əs/ adjective = បន្ត
(without a pause or interruption:)

e.g - 👉She is in continuous pain.
              នាងនៅតែបន្តគូស

👉 hotel/həʊˈtel/ noun = សណ្ឋាគារ
(a building where you pay to have a room to sleep in, and where you can sometimes eat meals:)

e.g - 👉at a hotel on the beach.
              នៅសណ្ឋាគារលើវាខ្សាច់

👉 seaside/ˈsiː.saɪd/ noun = មាត់សមុទ្រ
(the area near the sea, especially where people spend their holidays and enjoy themselves:)

e.g - 👉Let's go to the seaside at the weekend!
              តោះទៅមាត់សមុទ្រនៅចុងសប្តាហ៏

👉 stand /stænd/ verb = ឈរ
(to be in a vertical state or to put into a vertical state, especially (of a person or animal) by making the legs straight:)

e.g - 👉Granny says if she stands for a long time her ankles hurt.
              Granny និយាយថា ប្រសិនបើ នាងឈរយូ ជង្គង់នាង នឹងឈឺ

👉 rain /reɪn/ noun = ទឹកភ្លៀង
👉 rain /reɪn/ verb = ធ្លាក់ភ្លៀង
(If it rains, water falls from the sky in small drops:)

e.g - 👉It's raining hard/heavily
              កំពង់ធ្លាក់ភ្លៀងខ្លាំង

👉 shine /ʃaɪn/ verb = ជះពន្លឺ
(to send out or reflect light:)

e.g - 👉Is that light shining in your eyes?
              តើភ្លើងនោះ កំពង់ចាំងភ្នែកអ្នកឬ?

👉 eat /ʃaɪn/ verb = បរិភោគ, ញុាំ, សុី
(to put or take food into the mouth, chew it (= crush it with the teeth), and swallow it:)

e.g - 👉Do you eat meat?
              តើអ្នកញាំសាច់ឬ?

👉 ice /aɪs/ noun = ទឹកកក, ការ៉េម
(water that has frozen and become solid, or pieces of this:)

e.g - 👉The pond was covered in ice all winter.
              ទឹកត្រពាំងក្របដណ្តប់ដោយទឹកកកនៅរដូវត្រជាក់

👉 among /əˈmʌŋ/ preposition = ចំណោម
(in the middle of or surrounded by other things:)

e.g - 👉I saw a few familiar faces among the crowd.
              ខ្ញុំបានឃើញអ្នកមានមុខស្រដៀងគ្នាពីរ បីនាក់ក្នុងចំណោមហ្វូងមនុស្ស

👉 sand /sænd/ noun = ខ្សាច់
(a substance that consists of very small grains of rock, found on beaches and in deserts:)

e.g - 👉The children played all day in/on the sand.
              ក្មេងៗលេងខ្សាច់ពេញមួយថ្ងៃ

👉 sunshine/ˈsʌn.ʃaɪn/ noun = ពន្លឺព្រះអាទិត្យ
(the light and heat that come from the sun:)

e.g - 👉The children were out playing in the sunshine.
              ក្មេងៗចេញលេងខាងក្រៅ ក្រោមពន្លឺព្រះអាទិត្យ

👉 summer/ˈsʌm.ər/ noun = រដូវក្តៅ
(the season of the year between spring and autumn when the weather is warmest, lasting from June to September north of the equator and from December to March south of the equator:)

e.g - 👉We have breakfast on the balcony in (the) summer.
              ពួកយើងញាំអាហារព្រឹកនៅយ៉រផ្ទះនៅរដូវក្តៅ

👉 hot/hɒt/ adjective = ក្តៅ
(having a high temperature:)

e.g - 👉a hot, sunny day
              ថ្ងៃក្តៅ

👉 your /jɔːr/ determiner = របស់អ្នក
(belonging or relating to the person or group of people being spoken or written to:)

e.g - 👉Is this your bag?
              តើនេះជាកាបូបរបស់អ្នករឺ?

👉 song /sɒŋ/ noun = ចម្រៀង
(a usually short piece of music with words that are sung:)

e.g - 👉to sing a song
              ច្រៀងចម្រៀង

👉 mile /maɪl/ noun = ម៉ាយ
(a unit of distance equal to 1,760 yards or 1.6 kilometres:)

e.g - 👉The nearest town is ten miles away.
              ទីក្រុងជិតបំផុត ចម្ងាយ​ ដប់មាយ

(a very long way:) ឆ្ងាយណាស់

e.g - 👉He lives miles away on the other side of town.
              គាត់រស់នៅឆ្អាយណាស់នៅជាយក្រុងឯណោះ

👉 once /wʌns/ adverb = មួយដង
(one single time:)

e.g - 👉We have lunch together once a month.
              ពួកយើងញាំអាហារថ្ងៃត្រង់ជុំគ្នាមួយដងក្នុងមួយខែ

👉 sad /sæd/ adjective = មិនសម្បាយ, សោកស្តាយ, ទុក្ខព្រួយ
(unhappy or sorry:)

e.g - 👉I've just received some very sad news.
              ខ្ញុំទើបទទួលបានដំណឹងដែលមិនរីករាយមួយចំនួន

👉 uneatable /ʌnˈiː.tə.bəl/ adjective = មិនល្អគ្រប់គ្រាន់សម្រាប់បរិភោគ
(not suitable or good enough to eat:)

e.g - 👉We all complained bitterly about the uneatable breakfast.
              ពួកយើងបានប្តឹងយ៉ាងគំហុកអំពីអាហារពេលព្រឹកមិនល្អគ្រប់គ្រាន់សម្រាប់បរិភោគ

👉 undrinkable /ʌnˈdrɪŋ.kə.bəl/ adjective = មិនល្អគ្រប់គ្រាន់សម្រាប់ផឹក
(not suitable or good enough to drink:)

e.g - 👉 undrinkable coffee
              កាហ្វេមិនល្អគ្រប់គ្រាន់សម្រាប់ផឹក

👉 coffee/ˈkɒf.i/ noun = កាហ្វេ
(a dark brown powder with a strong flavour and smell that is made by crushing dark beans from a tropical bush and used to make a drink:)

e.g - 👉undrinkable coffee
              កាហ្វេមិនល្អគ្រប់គ្រាន់សម្រាប់ផឹក

👉 interesting/ˈɪn.tres.tɪŋ/ adjective = ដែលគួរអោយចាប់អារម្មណ៏
(Someone or something that is interesting keeps your attention because he, she, or it is unusual, exciting, or has a lot of ideas:)

e.g - 👉She's quite an interesting woman.
              នាងជាមនុស្សស្រីដែលគួរអោយចាប់អារម្មណ៏ខ្លាំងណាស់

👉 wine /waɪn/ noun = ស្រាទំពាំងបាយជូ
(an alcoholic drink that is usually made from grapes, but can also be made from other fruits or flowers. It is made by fermenting the fruit with water and sugar:)

e.g - 👉Would you like to see the wine list, sir?
              អ្នកចង់មើលបញ្ចីរាយនាមស្រារឺលោក?

👉 fly /flaɪ/ verb = ហោះ ហើរ
(When a bird, insect, or aircraft flies, it moves through the air:)

e.g - 👉The poor bird couldn't fly because it had a broken wing.
              បក្សីគួរអោយអាណិតមិនអាចហើរបានទេ ព្រោះបាក់ស្លាប

👉 motor /ˈməʊ.tər/ noun = ហោះ ហើរ
(a device that changes electricity or fuel into movement and makes a machine work:)

e.g - 👉The pump is powered by a small electric motor.
              បូមទឹកគឺប្រើកំលាំង ម៉ូទ័រអាគីសនីតូចមួយ

👉 motor /ˈməʊ.tər/ adjective [ before noun ] = រថយន្ត
(connected with cars or other vehicles that have engines and use roads:)

e.g - 👉 motor​ insurance
              ធានារ៉ាប់រង រថយន្តអាគីសនីតូចមួយ

👉 motor /ˈməʊ.tər/ verb = ជិះម៉ូតូ
(to drive:)

e.g - 👉I was just motoring along, minding my own business, when suddenly I was stopped by the police
              ខ្ញុំកំពង់តែជិះម៉ូតូសុខៗ រំពិចនោះប៉ូលិសបានខាត់ខ្ញុំ

👉 musical /ˈmjuː.zɪ.kəl/ adjective = តន្ត្រី
(related to or connected with music:)

e.g - 👉musical instruments
              ឧបករណ៏តន្ត្រី

👉 rubbish /ˈrʌb.ɪʃ/ noun = សំរាម
(waste material or things that are no longer wanted or needed:)

e.g - 👉I forgot to put the rubbish out this morning.
              ខ្ញុំភ្លេចដាក់សំរាម ខាងក្រៅព្រឹកមិញ

👉 above /əˈbʌv/ adverb, preposition = ខាងលើ
(in or to a higher position than something else:)

e.g - 👉There's a mirror above the sink.
              មានកញ្ចក់ខាងលើ កន្លែងលើងដៃ

👉 fast /fɑːst/ adjective = លឿន
(moving or happening quickly, or able to move or happen quickly:)

e.g - 👉a fastswimmer
              អ្នកហែលទឹកលឿន

👉 hate/heɪt/ verb = ស្អប់
(to dislike someone or something very much:)

e.g - 👉Kelly hates her teacher.
              Kelly​ស្អប់ គ្រូរបស់នាង

👉 dust /dʌst/ noun = ធូលី
(dry dirt in the form of powder that covers surfaces inside a building, or very small dry pieces of soil, sand, or other substances:)

e.g - 👉The furniture was covered in dust and cobwebs.
              គ្រឿងសង្ហារឹមប្រលាក់ទៅដោយធូលី និងសំបុកពីងពាង

👉 smell /smel/ verb = ហិតក្លិន, ធុំក្លិន
(to have a particular quality that others can notice with their noses:)

e.g - 👉My hands smell of onions.
              ដៃខ្ញុំមានក្លិន ខ្ទឹមបារាំង

👉 enjoyable/ɪnˈdʒɔɪ.ə.bəl/ adjective = ក្តីសុខ, រីករាយ
(An enjoyable event or experience gives you pleasure:)

e.g - 👉Thank you for a most enjoyable evening.
              អគុណសម្រាប់ការផ្តល់ភាពរីករាយ ពេលល្ងាច

👉 perhaps /pəˈhæps/ adv = ប្រហែល
(used to show that something is possible or that you are not certain about something:)

e.g - 👉He hasn't written to me recently - perhaps he's lost my address.
              គាត់មិនបានសរសេរមកខ្ញុំទេថ្មីៗនេះប្រហែល គាត់បាត់អាសយដ្ឋាន

👉 find /faɪnd/ verb = ស្វែងរក, រកឃើញ
(to discover, especially where a thing or person is, either unexpectedly or by searching, or to discover where to get or how to achieve something:)

e.g - 👉I couldn't find Andrew's phone number.
              ខ្ញុំមិនអាចរកឃើញ លេខទូរស័ព្ទ របស់ Andrew ទេ

👉 being /ˈbiː.ɪŋ/ noun = មានវត្តមាន,មានជីវិត, តាំងនៅ
(a person or thing that exists:)

e.g - 👉A nuclear war would kill millions of living beings.
              សង្គ្រៀម នុយក្លេអ៊ែ បានសម្លាប់មនុស្សដែលមានមានជិវិតរស់ រាប់លានអ្នក

👉 singer /ˈsɪŋ.ər/ noun = អ្នកចំរៀង
(a person who sings:)

e.g - 👉Are you a good singer?
              តើអ្នកជាចំរៀង រឺ?

👉 line /laɪn/ noun = ខ្សែរបន្ទាត់
(a long, thin mark on the surface of something:)

e.g - 👉a straight line
              ខ្សែរបន្ទាត់ ត្រង់

👉 so/səʊ/ adverb = ដូច្នេះ, ណាស់
(very, extremely, or to such a degree:)

e.g - 👉I think so
              ខ្ញុំគិតដូច្នេះ

e.g - 👉The house is so beautiful.
              ផ្ទះមួយនេះស្អាតខ្លាំងណាស់

👉 piano/piˈæn.əʊ/ noun = ព្យាណូ
(a large musical instrument with a row of black and white keys that are pressed to play notes:)

e.g - 👉I play the piano.
              ខ្ញុំលេងព្យាណូ

👉 comment /ˈkɒm.ent/ noun = ការសម្តែងមតិ
(something that you say or write that expresses your opinion:)

e.g - 👉She was asked about the pay increase but made no comment (= did not give an opinion).
              នាងបានសួរពីការចំណាយកើនឡើង តែគ្មានមតិ

👉 drink/drɪŋk/ noun = ភេសជ្ជះ
((an amount of) liquid that is taken into the body through the mouth:)

e.g - 👉They'd had no food or drink for two days.
              ពួកគេមិនបានបរិភោគអាហារ និងភេសជ្ជះ ពីរថ្ងៃហើយ

👉 drink/drɪŋk/ verb = ផឹក
(to take liquid into the body through the mouth:)

e.g - 👉He drank three glasses of water.
              គាត់ផឹក ទឹកអស់បីកែវ

👉 over /ˈəʊ.vər/ preposition = រំលង
(above or higher than something else, sometimes so that one thing covers the other; above:)

e.g - 👉The aeroplane is flyingover the mountains
              យន្តហោះ ហោះរំលង ភ្នំ

👉 piece /piːs/ noun = សន្លឹក, ដុំ, (ជាបំណែកនៃរបស់អ្វីមួយ)
(a part of something:)

e.g - 👉He cut the cake into six pieces.
              គាត់កាត់នំជា ប្រាំមួយដុំ

👉 paper/ˈpeɪ.pər/ noun = ក្រដាស
(thin, flat material made from crushed wood or cloth, used for writing, printing, or drawing on:)

e.g - 👉writing paper
              ក្រដាស សរសេរ

👉 desk /desk/ adverb = តុ
(a type of table that you can work at, often one with drawers:)

e.g - 👉school desk.
              តុ សាលា

👉 pronounce /prəˈnaʊns/ verb = បញ្ចេញសំលេង
(to say a word or a letter in a particular way:)

e.g - 👉How do you pronounce your surname?
              តើអ្នកបញ្ចេញសំលេង នាមត្រគោលអ្នកបែបណា?

👉 badly /ˈbæd.li/ adverb = អាក្រក់
(in a severe and harmful way:)

e.g - 👉It's hard to believe that he could treat his own family so badly.
              វាជារឿងដែលពីបាកជឿងណាស ដែលគាត់ធ្វើទុក្ខគ្រួសារខ្លួនយ៉ាងអាក្រក់ ថ្នាក់នេះ

👉 difficulty /ˈdɪf.ɪ.kəl.ti/ noun = ការលំបាក
(the fact of not being easy to do or understand:)

e.g - 👉We finished the job, but only with great difficulty.
              ការងារបានចប់ហើយ តែចប់ទៅដោយភាពលំបាក

👉 spell/spel/ verb = ប្រកប
(to form a word or words with the letters in the correct order:)

e.g - 👉How do you spell receive?
              តើអ្នកប្រកបពាក្យ receive បែបណា?
